President Chiang's New Year's Day Radio Address: The Essentials of National Self-Salvation and Saving the Nation (Continued)

To establish the foundation of national morality and spirit through the New Life Movement, and to promote the progress of material civilization through the National Economic Construction Movement. From the above, it can be seen that the New Life Movement is a revolutionary movement to enable the people of the whole country to establish personality and revive the nation. The so-called New Life is a rational life based on the spirit of "propriety, righteousness, integrity, and shame" and the principle of adapting to the needs of the times. We must earnestly complete the cultivation of morality and spirit from our daily lives. I hope that all compatriots across the country will strive unremittingly toward this goal. The ancients said, "If you can renovate yourself for one day, then do so day after day, and again day after day." This means that in our thoughts, spirit, and life, we must wash away all the stains of the old, so that we can be completely renewed, and then continue to seek renewal day by day, so as to cultivate the highest spirit and personality. Speaking of this, I would like to tell you, compatriots, that the "new" life we are going to implement, the so-called "new," is absolutely different from what is generally called "modern" or "fashionable." To implement the New Life Movement, we absolutely do not demand that all material enjoyments of what we eat, wear, live in, and use be novel, but that we constantly and thoroughly improve our living habits, actions, etc., so that our thoughts, morality, spirit, and personality are "new day after day," creating a new atmosphere of society and the whole country honoring propriety, valuing righteousness, abiding by integrity, and knowing shame. Once this new atmosphere is formed, a new society can be established. With a new society, a new country can naturally be established. Such a new country is a truly civilized, strong, and modern country. Guanzi said, "Propriety, righteousness, integrity, and shame are the four pillars of a country; if the four pillars are not upheld, the country will perish." We can also say from a positive perspective, "Propriety, righteousness, integrity, and shame are the four pillars of a country; if the four pillars are upheld, the country will be revived." Even a very small country can transform from poverty and weakness to wealth and strength in a short period and even dominate the world because it can understand propriety and righteousness and know integrity and shame. Our country is so large, with so many compatriots, and even more so with such a long and glorious history and a beautiful and great culture, and the intelligence and talent of our nation are no less than others. As long as we can restore the four pillars, there is no reason why we cannot immediately make the country rich and strong. As long as everyone works together with one heart and one mind and implements the New Life Movement consistently, and everyone becomes a modern citizen, making the atmosphere of society and the country new day by day and progressing day by day, we will certainly easily build a civilized and strong new country. Therefore, implementing the New Life Movement is the fundamental way for all our compatriots to save themselves and save the country.

Secondly, in addition to the New Life Movement, there is another most important thing for self-salvation and saving the country that we must all start from today and work especially hard to do. What is it? It is the "National Economic Construction Movement" that I proposed last year. This movement must be carried out simultaneously with the New Life Movement and complement each other. The purpose of the New Life Movement is to improve the people's living habits, thereby enhancing the people's morality and promoting the spirit of the nation, so as to improve the people's spiritual life and complete the spiritual construction of the country. The purpose of the National Economic Construction Movement is to develop the people's ability to work and create, increase the people's living materials, thereby improving the people's economic life, and complete the material construction of the country. Spiritual and material construction are interrelated, mutually influential, and mutually supportive. Neglecting one will make it difficult to succeed in both. Simultaneous progress will achieve twice the result with half the effort. Therefore, the National Economic Construction Movement and the New Life Movement must be carried out in tandem and will inevitably complement each other. We have already laid the foundation of national morality and spirit with the New Life Movement, and at the same time, we must complete the economic construction of the country with the National Economic Construction Movement and promote the progress of material civilization, so that the country can develop healthily, and so that we can save the country and revive the nation. Therefore, I hope that all compatriots across the country will remember at all times that these two movements are the most important central tasks for self-salvation and saving the country at present. Everyone must work together with one heart and one mind, strive for self-improvement, and unremittingly implement them. I believe that we can surely realize Dr. Sun Yat-sen's Three Principles of the People and complete the great cause of saving the country and reviving the nation.

Compatriots, you must understand that to save the country, we must have revolution, and revolution is to realize the Three Principles of the People. The Three Principles of the People takes "people's livelihood" as the center. What is the basis of people's livelihood? It is the economy. If the economy cannot develop, the people's livelihood cannot be improved. If the people's livelihood cannot be improved, the Three Principles of the People cannot be implemented. Therefore, to save the country and realize the Three Principles of the People, we must first strive for national economic construction to improve the people's livelihood, and the National Economic Construction Movement is the basic way for all our people to strive for national economic construction. I hope that our people across the country will work together. Now I will tell you about the implementation points and methods of the National Economic Construction Movement. First, revitalize agriculture. China has always been established on agriculture, and the people's livelihood and the country's survival are based on agriculture. Therefore, to engage in economic construction, the first important task is to revitalize agriculture. The method of revitalization is to adopt the method of rural cooperation, guided by cooperatives, and improve fertilizer production and seed selection, improve farming methods, invigorate rural finance, and streamline agricultural product marketing, to strive to increase agricultural production, with the initial goal of achieving self-sufficiency in food. In general, all daily necessities of the people across the country need no longer be purchased from foreign countries, in order to stop the drain and avoid the increasingly depleted national economy and people's livelihood. In order to achieve this goal, on the one hand, we must increase the production of agricultural raw materials to serve as the foundation for the development of national industries. At the same time, we must promote on-site processing and manufacturing, so that we can supply local needs at low prices, and further reduce transportation costs to supply various places. Second, encourage land reclamation and animal husbandry. Land is the source of all material production. To develop production, we must first "make the best use of the land." Therefore, all public and private wasteland must be reclaimed as much as possible. In areas with vast land and sparse population, we must encourage large-scale immigration, land reclamation, and livestock farming, and implement a military district land reclamation system, using collective labor to develop various agricultural benefits on a large scale. In addition, we must restore and increase rural by-products, such as livestock, horticulture, and fisheries. We should do our best to improve quality and increase production at the same time. Third, develop mineral resources. The Premier said, "The mining industry is the greatest cause of material civilization and economic progress." For decades, the reason why our material civilization and economic construction have not progressed is that the mining industry has not been developed, which is certainly the most direct and greatest reason. In the past, due to various obstacles in politics, economy, and society, the mining industry can be said to have achieved nothing. In the future, the government must adopt active protection and incentive policies, investigate the state of the mining industry, as well as the reasons that destroy and restrict the development of the mining industry, and improve various regulations concerning the mining industry, with the main purpose of reducing the burden, facilitating mining, encouraging mining investment, and supporting the independent operation and free development of mine owners. It is even more necessary to prohibit local governments and any special forces from controlling mining rights and competing with the people for profits. Moreover, because our country's financial resources are insufficient, we should welcome foreign investment to jointly develop China's mining industry. In this way, on the one hand, we can accommodate a large amount of labor and solve the problem of unemployment among compatriots, and at the same time, we can develop resources and promote the progress of material civilization. Fourth, promote compulsory labor. Compulsory labor is the most urgent way to implement national labor service to engage in national economic construction. Now our country is poor and does not have sufficient financial resources to complete various construction projects. Fortunately, we have many compatriots, and the labor of our compatriots is the most valuable economic driving force of the country, and the capital of all construction projects. As long as our people across the country can do their best to work, they can complete all the new construction projects that benefit the country and the people, save themselves and save the country, and fulfill their responsibilities to the country. The ancients said, "Educating the people with labor enriches them" and "Worry and labor invigorate the country," which is exactly the same as what we call labor service. I hope that compatriots across the country will understand this meaning together, support the government in implementing the compulsory labor system, and actively participate in voluntary labor. At least, we must first engage in basic work of local economic construction such as local development of transportation, water conservancy, forestry, and land reclamation with the efforts of local compatriots. In addition to the compulsory labor system, the government should simultaneously implement a military labor policy, using the labor of the army to supplement the shortcomings of the compulsory labor in various places. I believe that all construction projects in various places, if they receive the help of the army, will definitely achieve twice the result with half the effort. Fifth, promote industry. If industry cannot develop, material civilization cannot progress and economic life cannot be satisfactory. Therefore, in addition to vigorously promoting agriculture, forestry, and mining, the most important thing is to strive for the development of industry. Our old-fashioned handicraft industry has already declined, and the new-style mechanical industry has not yet developed due to the oppression of foreign economies. Now, to seek ways to revitalize the declining industry, enrich the country, and enrich the people, on the one hand, we should promote simple rural industries and simple industries for processing and manufacturing agricultural products, and operate them in the countryside or its vicinity according to the cooperative system, in order to seek close connection and mutual development between agriculture and industry. On the one hand, the government should protect and reward general industries separately, in order to achieve self-sufficiency in national industrial products. At the same time, it is necessary to establish labor-capital adjustment agencies to fairly mediate all disputes between labor and capital and increase the interests of both parties. Such agencies must be given the power of final mandatory execution, in order to protect the safety of enterprises and the work of laborers. Sixth, adjust consumption. In our country, where production capacity is weak and all production industries are backward, various living materials are extremely scarce, and most of them must rely on foreign countries. Therefore, it creates economic septicemia in which rural funds are concentrated in cities and then transferred to foreign countries, so that the rural economy is on the verge of bankruptcy, all industries are declining at the same time, and the most serious economic crisis is that the country is becoming increasingly poor. The only way to remedy this is to treat both the symptoms and the root cause. On the one hand, we must make the greatest efforts in the positive aspect to fundamentally increase the national production capacity and develop the national production industry. At the same time, we must make the greatest efforts in the negative aspect to save consumption as much as possible and adjust supply and demand. Compatriots, you must know that saving consumption can be done with just a change of mind, which is much easier than increasing production. However, this matter has the same effect on saving the country as increasing production. With such an easy, practical, and effective thing, how can we not strive to implement it? In short, in the future, we must strive to save consumption, adjust supply and demand, and prevent the outflow of funds from the mainland and rural areas, and further achieve the balance of foreign trade imports and exports. Seventh, streamline freight transportation. The basic condition for streamlined freight transportation is convenient transportation. Therefore, we must develop road transportation throughout the country as much as possible, improve the methods of water and land freight transportation, and at the same time, establish public warehouses and marketing agencies for major agricultural products such as cotton, wheat, rice, silk, and tea in various important areas, in order to store and transfer them. Eighth, adjust finance. Finance is the lifeline of the economy. If finance loses its normal state, all industries will suffer adverse effects. Therefore, adjusting finance is the most basic and most important task of national economic construction. When it comes to adjusting financial methods, it lies in encouraging private savings, invigorating the flow of funds, and responding to the requirements of the times. The government must implement a sound monetary policy, and the people across the country must absolutely trust the government and unanimously support its implementation.

The above eight items are the main tasks of the National Economic Construction Movement. Many of them are very simple, practical, and easy to do, and anyone can do them. If the people across the country can consistently follow these principles and do them practically, I believe that not only can our own lives become stable as a result, but also the entire economic national crisis can be quickly broken through, and the country will gradually move towards the realm of wealth and strength. Otherwise, the national economy will have no way to be built, the people's livelihood problem will not be solved, and everyone will only become poorer day by day, and even the majority of the people will suffer from hunger and cold, and their lives will not be stable. Then, society and the country will only become more chaotic and dangerous, and cannot be saved. Therefore, everyone must deeply recognize that this movement is the most important task for self-salvation and saving the country at present. From today onwards, we must work together to strive for advancement and earnestly implement it. At the same time, we must support and urge the government to do its best to implement it. In this way, our country can be immediately saved by these basic tasks. Everyone must understand that our intelligence and talent are as sound as foreigners, and our population is larger than any other country. Things that they do in five or ten years can be accomplished in one year if we work together with one heart and one mind. Therefore, we are not afraid of how poor or weak the country is, or how dangerous it is, but only that we have intelligent brains and great strength, but we are unwilling to use them and do not know how to develop them to the fullest. We are only afraid that our compatriots still do not have the concept of the country and the nation, do not understand their responsibilities, do not fulfill their obligations, do not abide by discipline, and cannot unite as a group. Especially for everything, we cannot do it practically. If we do not do it, of course nothing will succeed. If we can do it, I think there is nothing truly difficult in the world. Now that the country has reached such a critical point of survival, to be able to save ourselves and save the country, the only way is for our 400 million compatriots to promote the New Life Movement on the one hand, so that everyone becomes a modern citizen, in order to build the foundation of the national spirit. On the other hand, we must work together to promote the National Economic Construction Movement, so that everyone can fulfill the obligation of labor and develop the nation's production capacity, building the foundation of the country's material. Thus, these two movements, which emphasize both mind and matter, and combine substance and function, are the most important methods for implementing the Three Principles of the People, and the most practical way for all our compatriots to save themselves and save the country. I hope that everyone will make great vows from today onwards and strive to implement them. In particular, people of the intellectual class must take on the responsibility of leadership, lead by example, and advocate with all their strength, so that the people across the country will follow this path and work together to do the work of self-salvation and saving the country. Our 400 million compatriots are all descendants of the same ancestor, all of the same flesh and blood, and should have the love of brothers and sisters. Everyone's interests are closely related, and we share the same fate. At this critical moment of the country's life and death, the only way is to be of one heart and one mind, to be self-reliant and self-strengthening, to unite sincerely, to support the central government, and to strive forward towards the overall goal of saving the country. We are not afraid of any foreign aggression, and we can break through any danger. The Three Principles of the People will surely be realized by our hands, the Republic of China will surely be saved, and the Chinese nation will surely be revived. In this way, we individuals can be said to be modern citizens, fulfilling the important responsibility of carrying on the past and opening up the future for the citizens of the Republic of China, and we can be worthy of our ancestors and comfort the spirit of our Father of the Nation, Dr. Sun Yat-sen, in heaven. What I have said to our compatriots across the country today is these few words. I hope that all of you will strive together and actively work hard to achieve them. I wish you all health and success, and I wish our Republic of China long live, long live, long live! (End)

Current Commentary

Broadcasting and China's Unification

— Star

On New Year's Day this year, Chairman Lin Zichao of the National Government and Premier Chiang Kai-shek of the Executive Yuan broadcast their New Year's speeches to 400 million people across China and to various ethnic groups in Asia via the Central Broadcasting Radio Station. On that day, dozens of radio broadcasting stations across China simultaneously broadcast these speeches. Wherever Chinese people are found, whether in border areas or in Southeast Asia, they can use this new scientific tool to receive the sound transmitted from Nanjing in the air, as if gathering in the same room with China's political leaders. This phenomenon, its benefit to national unity and the effectiveness of national unification, can be said to be immeasurable.

The unification of a country depends on the people having a unified consciousness, a unified understanding, and a unified determination. The most effective tools for building this kind of unified psychology are news media and broadcasting. After the war, emerging countries spared no effort in promoting nationalism through these two tools, making full use of them for effective control. However, news media are not as powerful as radio in mobilizing national sentiment, because seeing people through writing is not as good as communicating with people through language. Moreover, there are not many literate people in China, and transportation is inconvenient. Disseminating an opinion or order throughout China cannot be done immediately through newspapers. Radio is not limited by time and space. Once a word is spoken, the whole country can hear it. Joy, anger, sorrow, and happiness can all be aroused by the speaker's effect, resulting in the direct reaction of the listeners. China has a vast territory, and people's thoughts and opinions vary. To make the people aware of the country and the government, and to make the people aware of the ways to work for the country, radio broadcasting should be used more actively in the future, so that Nanjing's largest broadcasting station in Asia can fully play its function in building a unified national psychology and a strong national consciousness.

Looking broadly at the efforts and successes of various countries in broadcasting in recent years, after the Soviet revolution, radio was used as a tool to build a new civilization and promote a new political and economic system. Moscow has a broadcasting station ten times larger than Nanjing's. Observers say that Hitler's victory in Germany was thanks to the radio broadcasting industry. Even in the democratic United States, the president makes active use of radio broadcasting at all times. Whenever Roosevelt has political opinions to express, he instructs hundreds of radio stations across the United States to simultaneously broadcast his speeches to the people. China's Nanjing radio station has considerable power, but having a large radio station without a sufficient number of radios, or having radios without valuable programs, is still of no avail. To achieve psychological unification in China, improving and expanding the radio broadcasting industry is a pressing task at present.

Five-Nation Representatives Gather in London: Naval Conference Reopens Today

Quantitative Restrictions Difficult to Compromise

London - The Naval Conference in London, which adjourned on December 20 last year, is scheduled to reconvene on the 6th of this month. The delegations from the United States, Japan, and Italy previously spent the New Year elsewhere and have now returned here. As no extensive preparations are required for the resumption of the conference, most of the representatives will be able to take time off in the next two days to play golf and relax. All the delegations believe that the negotiations after the resumption of the conference must be conducted actively. "The quantitative restriction agreement is likely to be established, and must be determined as soon as possible. If it cannot be established, then the issue of qualitative restrictions should be discussed. It is generally believed that if no agreement can be reached, the Naval Conference will end quickly," it is said. (Havas dispatch on the 4th)

London - The Naval Disarmament Conference is scheduled to reopen on the 6th as planned. The chair will be taken by the new Foreign Secretary Eden. During the adjournment, no sign of compromise was found, so there is fear that the final breakup will be faster than expected. (Domei dispatch on the 4th)

Mrs. Rogers has requested the State Department to find ways to control the competition of Japanese rayon in the Philippines, especially Japanese rayon transshipped from China to the Philippines and rayon manufactured by Japanese merchants in China. Roosevelt's Remarks Aimed at Promoting Peace

Opposing Aggression, Emphasizing the Actions of Italy and Japan, Revising International Treaties, Door Not Closed

Washington - Diplomatic circles and the State Department today generally believe that President Roosevelt's message is the strongest statement on foreign affairs by an American president since President Wilson asked Congress to declare war on Germany. It is reported that President Roosevelt's remarks were made to promote neutrality legislation. Diplomatic circles believe that what the President meant was the actions of Italy against Abyssinia, Japan against China, and Germany's rearmament, and publicly proposed the union of Western Hemisphere countries to seek world peace. (Kokumin dispatch on the 4th)

London - Observers here today believe that President Roosevelt, through his message to Congress, has facilitated the possibility of passing an oil embargo against Italy, and has encouraged countries that do not engage in aggression. A government spokesman said, "President Roosevelt's message, while avoiding disputes, also clearly declares that the United States will use its enormous power in the world to oppose countries seeking new conquests." It is also believed here that the President has not closed the door to revising treaties by peaceful means. (Kokumin dispatch on the 4th)

Paris - A government spokesman declared today that he fully agreed with President Roosevelt's message, calling it "a call for calm reason." French newspapers have given good reviews to President Roosevelt's criticism of dictatorial politics. (Kokumin dispatch on the 4th)

Differing Perspectives from Various Nations

Rome Anxious, German Press Critical, Paris Expresses Sympathy

Paris - According to sources in Rome, the Italian government fears that President Roosevelt's speech signals a potential reduction in US oil supplies to Italy. Italy relies heavily on US oil to continue its war efforts. A reduction to pre-war levels would significantly hinder Italy. However, many Italians believe that if the US acknowledges the principle of supplying warring nations with a certain amount of gasoline, it will be difficult to limit that quantity. (Reuters, 5th)

Rome - Official circles have made no statement regarding President Roosevelt's address to Congress. However, the general sentiment here is one of agreement. President Roosevelt clearly stated that kerosene would continue to be exported within normal peacetime limits, making a global oil embargo difficult to achieve. Furthermore, news from London indicates that the British government does not intend to be the first to advocate for stricter sanctions at the League of Nations. This news strengthens hopes that an oil embargo will not materialize. Moreover, US oil imports account for only one-sixth of Italy's total kerosene imports. Currently, Italy's kerosene supply, combining domestic reserves and existing orders, is ample enough to cope with future events. Even if consumption exceeds normal levels due to unforeseen circumstances, normal US imports would suffice. (Havas, 4th)

Berlin - Various circles here have criticized President Roosevelt's address to Congress. The semi-official Diplomatic and Political Correspondence stated, "The US desire not to profit from other nations' wars aligns with Germany's stance since the outbreak of the Italo-Abyssinian War." Political figures emphasized the new Neutrality Act to be discussed after Congress reconvenes, calling it a new concept of wartime neutrality, treating all belligerents equally. Regarding President Roosevelt's statement about "dictators of foreign lands, who enslave their people and drive them onto the battlefield," newspapers refrained from praise or criticism. However, the Nazi Party organ, "Angriff," commented, "President Roosevelt's tone suggests genuine moral conscience, perhaps possible under the American democratic banner. However, dictatorial nations are merely bombs threatening the world. England and America consistently compare Stalin of Soviet Russia, Hitler of Germany, and Mussolini of Italy to those who champion democratic ideals, claiming they are diametrically opposed. This view is widespread, proving that England and America still do not understand the true nature of political systems outside their own framework." (Reuters, 4th)

London - A spokesman for the Berlin Foreign Office criticized President Roosevelt's address to Congress, which implied that some nations are destroying democratic public opinion and displaying dictatorial aggression. He stated that Roosevelt's remarks were not directed at Germany, as Germany had done nothing to warrant such comments. He further stated that Germany's dictatorship is completely different from others, implying that Roosevelt was thinking of other nations when he made his statement. (Reuters, 4th)

Berlin - President Roosevelt's address to Congress has angered the German press. The Angriff newspaper called the speech ridiculous, demonstrating the US's superficial understanding of dictatorial nations. It also claimed that the Nazi government had reached an understanding with Poland, relinquishing all territorial claims against France, and had reached a naval understanding with Britain. (Reuters, 5th)

Paris - The French are delighted by President Roosevelt's criticism of Mussolini's dictatorship in his address to Congress. They are now questioning the influence of Roosevelt's statement on Geneva's decision regarding an oil embargo against Italy. The newspaper "Le Temps" believes the pro-sanctions faction will become more assertive. "Journal des Débats" suggests the implementation of the American Neutrality Act will turn the Kellogg-Briand Pact into a laughingstock, greatly benefiting nations whose primary industry is war. (Reuters, 5th)

Paris - The newspaper "Le Temps" recently commented on President Roosevelt's message to Congress, stating, "In future global conflicts, one cannot reasonably expect the US to intervene and cooperate with other nations defending justice and freedom, as it did during the European War. Furthermore, in accordance with the spirit of wartime neutrality, nations fighting to protect their rights and independent existence, as well as those seeking to conquer others and engage in aggression, cannot rely on the US to supply munitions or essential raw materials. This situation will greatly alter all future wars of defense or aggression. Under these circumstances, all nations must plan carefully in terms of domestic industry, so that in times of crisis, those previously reliant on US products must find alternative solutions. This will encourage nations to pursue self-sufficiency. Moreover, with US raw material supplies unreliable during wartime, raw material-producing countries, especially Soviet Russia, stand to benefit." (Havas, 4th)

New US Neutrality Act More Flexible

Grants President Broad Powers to Act Based on Aggressor's Actions

Washington - Representative McReynolds, Chairman of the House Foreign Affairs Committee, yesterday introduced a new Neutrality Act to the House of Representatives, proposing amendments to the current law to make it a permanent neutrality law. According to political observers here, President Roosevelt's interpretation and implementation of this law can be gleaned from his address to Congress yesterday. The new Neutrality Act proposed by McReynolds grants the President broad "discretionary" powers, unlike the strict "mandatory" nature of the current law (referring to measures that must be taken). According to the new law, items not purely for war but usable in war, such as kerosene, copper, and cotton, should be prohibited from being transported to belligerent nations, to be decided by the President's discretion. The President's ability to use this power to expand the list of embargoed items is intended to "ensure American security, maintain American neutrality, and prevent the expansion and prolongation of war." Once international conflicts occur, the US President will have the power to act at his discretion and the flexibility to adjust his actions, which is of utmost importance. In his address, the President harshly criticized "aggressive dictatorships," stating that these nations alone bear the responsibility for brewing war. Conversely, he stated that nations that "consistently uphold democracy" are those who cherish peace. Upon careful examination of the President's words, it is feared that war may break out in both Europe and the Far East, thus revealing the future "aggressor nations" in advance. From this perspective, once an international war occurs, President Roosevelt will distinguish between the severity of the belligerents' responsibilities as the standard for the scope of the Neutrality Act's implementation. For aggressor nations, all provisions of the Neutrality Act will be strictly enforced without leniency. For attacked nations, only the "mandatory" or prescribed measures of the Neutrality Act will be implemented, and not others. (Havas, 4th)

Paris - After receiving detailed information about President Roosevelt's address to Congress, responsible parties here have commented extensively on the new Neutrality Act under discussion in the US Congress. These individuals value the law itself, rather than Roosevelt's speech. Firstly, the law demonstrates the American people's strong desire to maintain neutrality and protect peace with all their might. Secondly, viewing the provisions of the law, the traditional American concept of freedom of the seas may be revised. If the law is passed, it will grant the President new privileges, allowing him to expand the list of embargoed items beyond the current ban on munitions, including items the President deems prolonging war for belligerent nations. Therefore, the authorities may implement a naval blockade, extending the effectiveness of the blockade to their own ships. This result would make the Neutrality Act effective. And if this becomes a reality, it may have a significant impact on actions in Geneva, as the implementation of Article 16 of the League of Nations Covenant may also adopt a naval blockade to deal with aggressor nations. However, regarding this matter, Britain has not yet dared to attempt it lightly, lest upholding the American argument for freedom of the seas lead to disputes between the two countries. But if the new American Neutrality Act is completed, this difficulty can be resolved. However, if the League decides to postpone the implementation of certain embargo measures, the American President's planned embargo measures against both belligerent parties may be affected. The above is a general expression of opinion from official circles regarding the new Neutrality Act, refraining from commenting on its relationship to the Italo-Abyssinian War. The current US Neutrality Act, established on September 1st last year, will expire at the end of February this year, stipulating only the embargo of war materials to belligerent nations. Representative McReynolds, Chairman of the House Foreign Affairs Committee, introduced the new bill to the House on the 3rd (details already seen in yesterday's telegram). (Havas, 5th)

After its passage, the method of payment will be discussed. Mr. Vincent's plan does not specify the method of payment, but only requests the payment of the bonus. The 21-member Pittman Bonus Act Committee will meet on Monday to decide whether to abandon or persist with inflation, or postpone this dispute until after the Bonus Act is passed. The President is prepared to use his past achievements as the standard for his re-election. It is understood that the President intends to remain silent until the summer campaign begins, then present his new proposals to the voters, allowing them to freely choose whether to re-elect Roosevelt to continue reforms or elect his political opponents to overthrow his "New Deal." (National Telegram, 4th)

US Private Company Profits, Supplies Military Aircraft to Bolivia

Indicted Last Summer for Violations, Neutrality Act a Litmus Test

Washington - The US-based Stanba Aircraft Company previously disregarded the prohibition and sold four bomber aircraft to Bolivia (when the Chaco War had not yet ceased, the US government explicitly prohibited the transport of all military supplies to both Bolivia and Paraguay). Ostensibly, they were intended for use on the New Orleans-Mexico air route. After the aircraft were shipped out, the company ceased operations to evade responsibility. At the time, the State Department was caught off guard and unable to intercept them. Later, after obtaining the consent of the Peruvian government, it was agreed to detain the aircraft when they passed through that country. This happened last summer. Subsequently, the judicial authorities conducted an investigation into the case, learning that Stanba Company was a subsidiary of the well-known Curtiss Aircraft Factory. According to the State Department, the Bolivian consul in New York had participated in the sale. The Curtiss factory authorities were then prosecuted. The factory authorities refused to answer some important questions, and the State Department and the Department of Justice wanted to ask the Bolivian consul to testify, but were refused, resulting in a deadlock in the lawsuit. According to the US-Bolivian treaty, the US government cannot compel Bolivian civil servants to appear in court to testify. State Department officials now hope that the Bolivian government will assist, so that the truth of the case can be revealed. The State Department believes that the nature of this case is important, and is related to various countries in South America and Europe, and can be a litmus test for the new Neutrality Act. Generally, it is believed that if American companies violate the Neutrality Act and the American government cannot obtain the testimony of foreign civil servants residing in the United States, it will be difficult for the implementation of the Neutrality Act to be effective. (Havas, 4th)

Repeated Violations of Wartime Laws, Over 200,000 Italian Troops in East Africa

Once this report arrives, a response plan will be decided. (Havas, 4th)

Science Talks - Edited by the China Science Society

Talking About Red Leaves (Continued)

— Zhang Chu

The red leaves seen in spring are mostly newly grown, tender leaves. Common examples include plants of the Acer, Rhododendron, and Pistacia genera. According to most scholars, the purpose of these tender leaves turning red is to shield them from excessively strong sunlight, thereby protecting the delicate tissues. This is because while sunlight is a necessary driving force for plant life, each plant has its own specific light requirement, that is, a certain optimum. If the light is too strong and exceeds the optimum, or if the light is too weak and falls short of the optimum, it can be harmful to the plant. The reason why trees in the spring often have red or light red new leaves is to prevent the penetration of excessively strong light, so as to avoid the decomposition of chlorophyll. What about the red leaves in autumn? There are two exactly opposite theories to explain why leaves turn red in the fall: the first theory states that the red anthocyanins have two functions: (1) the red color can shield the plant from harmful, strong light, allowing chemical changes within the leaf to proceed smoothly without obstruction, which is the same as the explanation for red leaves in spring. (2) The red color can absorb a lot of heat from the red rays of light, increasing the temperature inside the leaf and promoting chemical changes. In other words, it allows the important chemical compounds inside the leaf to be completely broken down and transported to the stem for storage, so as to avoid being lost with the fallen leaves in autumn and winter. However, another theory is completely different. This theory states that red leaves are merely a physiological response of the plant to seasonal changes, and do not bring any benefit to the plant itself. There is really no great significance as to why it is like this. The reason why they release beautiful colors before withering is like the afterglow of the setting sun, which is completely different from the purpose of flowers displaying beautiful colors to attract insects. It can be said that there is no definitive conclusion as to which of the two theories is right or wrong.

People often confuse red leaves with maple leaves, and almost assume that all red leaves are maple leaves. In fact, the leaves of many plants turn red, not just maple leaves. Pistacia chinensis, Acer buergerianum, Acer palmatum, Acer japonicum, Rhaphiolepis indica, Sapium sebiferum, Nandina domestica, Celtis sinensis, Ulmus parvifolia, Betula, and others are also common tree species with red leaves in the autumn. We will now present several species and simply illustrate the shapes of their leaves, so that you will not think of them as maple leaves when you see red leaves in the future.

(1) Maple

The maple tree, also known as fragrant maple or Liquidambar formosana, belongs to the Hamamelidaceae family. This is the true maple tree. It often grows into a large tree with alternate leaves. The fruit is a drooping, spiky ball.

(2) Trident Maple

Also known as Acer buergerianum, it belongs to the Aceraceae family. Farmers often plant it as a hedge. It rarely grows into a large tree. It is most easily confused with (1), but the leaves of the trident maple are opposite and the fruit is a winged fruit, which are very different from maple.

(3) Chinese Tallow Tree

Sapium sebiferum is quite common in Jiangsu and Zhejiang. The leaves are heart-shaped and easily recognizable. When its fruit splits open, you can see three white, waxy-coated seeds. The oil extracted from the seeds can be used to make candles, soap, and for lighting lamps. The leaves can also be used as a black silk dye.

(4) Indian Hawthorn

Indian Hawthorn is often planted in cemeteries. The tree shape is rounded and beautiful. The leaves are thick and have fine thorns on the edges. In autumn and winter, some of the leaves turn red, which is extremely bright.

(5) Chinese Pistache

This is a compound leaf. The base of the leaflets is skewed and asymmetrical. In spring, the newly emerged leaves are as red and bright as the head of an oriole. The tender leaves are fragrant and can be used as a substitute for tea. Some people pickle them with salt and sell them as Chinese Pistache tea. In Shandong, it is called the "kai" tree. It is said that the statue of Confucius in the Confucius Temple in Qufu is made of this wood.

(6) Finally, let me introduce the most beautiful red leaf, which is the Acer palmatum. It also belongs to the Aceraceae family. It has winged fruits and seven-lobed leaves. The new leaves and autumn leaves turn red. Pressed and displayed in books or framed, they are absolutely beautiful. There is also a type with five-lobed leaves, which is also quite beautiful.

Page 8

Mediterranean Region: Past and Present of British Policy

Italy Decides to Move Forward with Current Policy

Rome - Senate President Volpi, in a speech at the International Political Science Society in Milan today, stated that in the past, Britain, in view of the development of French and Russian forces in the Mediterranean, had sought to unite with Italy to jointly resist France and Russia. Since the European War, the combined French and Russian forces in the Mediterranean have declined, and British policy has also changed accordingly. This situation has become increasingly apparent, especially after the success of the Fascist revolution and the further consolidation of Italy's position due to the Franco-Italian understanding. Volpi further stated that Italy is determined to complete its current policy, and is not concerned about British opposition. He also said, "The new Italy is a political entity in the Mediterranean that cannot be suppressed. Italy is a country with 44 million people and must move forward. Who can force it to give up its progress? It should be known that Italy's aspirations for Africa do not harm British interests. This has been repeatedly and clearly expressed by the leaders of the Italian government. Italy does not want to weaken Britain's position, because this kind of attempt would affect the situation in Europe and would be harmful to Italy." (Havas, 5th)

Japan Establishes New Legations in Abyssinia and Egypt

Tokyo - The Ministry of Foreign Affairs has already started its first project of this year, establishing legations in Abyssinia and Egypt on New Year's Day. According to a telegram from Suzuki, the acting minister to Abyssinia, the legation in Addis Ababa is temporarily located in the Imperial Hotel. As soon as the Abyssinian Emperor returns to the capital from the front lines, he will perform the audience ceremony as acting minister. As for the legation to Egypt, it has been decided that the Consul General in Alexandria, Amagi, will temporarily act as minister. Japan's Fiscal Panic

National and Local Debts Increase Annually, Lame Finances Lead to Lame Economy

Hwa-Lien News Agency Special Article - The stability or panic of a country's finances is a reflection of the good or bad economic situation of that country. From Japan's fiscal panic, we can see the crisis in the Japanese economy.

Since the September 18 Incident in 1931, as a result of Japan's unreasonable expansion of its finances, the financial situation has been exhausted to the extreme. Looking at the newly annexed Manchuria, it is suffering from a lack of investment. It is said that in order to restore order, the special expenses used in the past four years have further increased the financial instability of the Japanese state.

Speaking of national debt, it has changed from 5.055 billion yen in September 1931 to 9.7644 billion yen in August last year. If we add the 50 million yen in treasury securities and the 528 million yen in rice securities, then, in the past four years, just in terms of the central government's public debt, it has increased from 6.187 billion yen to 10.342 billion yen, an increase of 4.155 billion yen.

Looking at local debt, it was 1.6885 billion yen in 1931, and it increased to 2.4447 billion yen in June last year, that is, an increase of 76.2%. That is to say, the total amount of public debt in Japan's finances has increased to more than 5 billion yen. This more than 5 billion yen of public debt is forcibly distributed to banks and then transferred to the already unsustainable burden of the Japanese toiling masses. At the end of 1931, the national debt amount stored in the bank's treasury was only 1.811 billion yen, but in July of last year, it suddenly increased to 4.146 billion yen. Adding the 443 million yen in local debt and the huge amount of capital invested in national debt by insurance companies, the number is even more considerable.

Looking at the deposits in Japan's deposit department, they have indeed increased in recent years. However, the increase in both new and old deposits has been used by the national treasury to increase national debt. Even the government's various corporate bonds have been included in the treasury of the deposit department. The total deposit amount is about 3.2 billion yen, but the capital used for government securities is 3.5 billion yen. Even the reserves have been misappropriated. In short, the public debt accumulated in the treasuries of Japanese financial groups is about 12.8 billion yen. As for the majority of the funds of Japanese banks, they are also absorbed into other securities. In July last year, the investment in stocks and bonds of Japanese private bank companies was 2.404 billion yen, credit companies 596 million yen, and insurance companies 800 million yen. It is estimated that two-thirds of Japan's entire financial capital is solidified in various securities. The excessive amount of securities illustrates the urgency of Japan's finances. Moreover, in general, the value of bonds indicates a continuous decline. There is also the expansion of Japanese banknotes and currency. To give an example, in September 1921, the amount of silver banknotes issued was 1.054 billion yen. By July last year, it had increased to 1.202 billion yen. The amount of banknotes issued by the Fresh Silver Bank increased from 100 million yen to 147 million yen. The amount issued by the Taiwan Bank increased from 44 million yen to 45 million yen. This uneven increase is the focus of the conflict of interest among Japanese financial giants themselves.

Before the compilation of the Japanese fiscal budget for this year, Finance Minister Takahashi insisted on no longer increasing public debt and adopted the "dualism of military and financial resources." However, as a result, out of the total expenditure of 2.278 billion yen in the general accounting budget, the army and navy military expenses accounted for 1.059 billion yen, that is, 46.5% of the total expenditure. That is, the military expenditure for this year has increased by 38 million yen compared to last year. On the other hand, the expenses of the Ministry of Agriculture and Forestry, which are frequently in bankruptcy panic and need to be rescued, were 123 million yen in Showa 9 (1934), but decreased to 93 million yen last year (Showa 10), and further decreased to 90 million yen this year.

In this way, Japan's lame finances are further promoting the transformation of a lame economy. Only a small part of the military demand industry has received a little bit of profit. The majority of the rural economy, small and medium-sized industrial and commercial operators, and the toiling masses are further trapped in a quagmire of hardship. Japan's fiscal panic has fully pointed out the crisis in the Japanese economy, explaining that Japan's internal strength is really empty to the extreme.

New Year's Day Reception: Kuling British Concession

The Lushan Administration Director and the British Consul in Hankou Jointly Signed 14 Articles of Agreement for Return

Nanchang Correspondence - Lushan is located in the middle reaches of the Yangtze River, only 45 li from Jiujiang. You can take a car from Jiujiang directly to Lianhua Cave and then take a sedan chair to climb the mountain. Transportation is convenient. The mountain has nine layers, and the peaks are inserted into the sky. It is vast and majestic, almost unparalleled in the southeast. Kuling is located in the northwest of Lushan. The scenery is quiet and is considered a giant. Since Chinese and foreign people gathered to escape the summer heat, various constructions have been modernized. Western-style houses stand all over the mountains. As for the process of leasing it to foreigners, it can be traced back to the eleventh year of Guangxu (1885 AD). An English missionary, Lide Li, happened to travel here and was extremely envious of its beautiful scenery. He then tried to purchase land in the Changheng area of ​​Kuling from the Chinese to build houses and roads. When the local gentry learned about it, the interference was ineffective. It was not until the twenty-first year of Guangxu that the lease was officially established. The British then focused on operations, using the excuse of escaping the summer heat to expand it. In the thirtieth year of Guangxu, they re-signed the expanded lease. As a result, the British also established the Kuling Company to exercise political power. By this time, the British had formed a mature lease in Kuling.

In the fifteenth year of the Republic of China, the Revolutionary Army recovered the Yangtze River area and recovered part of the police power. In the twenty-second year, the Lushan Administration was reorganized, and all matters progressed rapidly. The British expressed their intention to return the leased summer resort. At the beginning of August in the twenty-third year, the director of the Lushan Administration, Chiang Chih-cheng, and the British Consul General in Hankou, He Lide, began discussing the return method. Later, He Lide was transferred back to his country, so the current Consul General in Hankou, Moose, continued the negotiations. After several twists and turns, the draft agreement was signed in September of the twenty-fourth year and approved by the Chinese and British governments. On December 30, Director Chiang and the British Consul Moose signed the original agreement, with a total of 14 articles. The content is extremely fair, and the interests of Chinese and foreign residents have been taken into consideration. It is completely managed by our country. The handover procedures were completed on New Year's Day. The Lushan Administration will also move to the original site of the Kuling Company. It is also heard that the Central Government has decided to allocate 100,000 yuan each year for the Lushan business, planning to actively build it. (January 2)

After finishing, he will leave Peiping for Tianjin to inspect the Peiping-Liaoning and Tientsin-Pukou Railways. After finishing the inspection in Qingdao, if time permits, he will visit the Longhai and Peiping-Hankou Railways, or he will transfer to Hankou from Xuzhou. The time is tentatively set for two weeks. If there is not enough time, the Longhai and Peiping-Hankou Railways will be left for future inspection. Chang has just taken office and is not very familiar with the situation of the various railways, so he decided to go to the various railways to conduct on-site inspections. The Railway Department's work plan for this year is to quickly complete the Yuehan and Rongyu Railways within the shortest possible time. However, there are many mountains on the Rongyu Line, and it is quite difficult to build railways. The government had this plan in the twenty-third year of the Republic of China. At that time, it was surveyed once, but this matter has not been realized. Now, all aspects of the situation have changed. If you want to build a railway, you still need to re-survey. After the survey is completed, construction can begin." (3rd)

Yuehan Railway: Engineering of the Zhuzhou-Shaoguan Section

Track-laying South of Hengyang Extends to Chenzhou Border; Roadbed in Chenping, Chenzhou, Already Taking Shape

All projects of the Hengyang Communication and Yuehan Railway Zhuzhou-Shaoguan section were rushed day and night in the year of the twenty-fourth, and the work was very tense. Sixteen difficult mountain tunnels on the entire line have been completed one after another. At the provincial border between Hunan and Guangdong, there are five huge steel-concrete arch bridges. Due to the inconvenience of transporting materials, progress has been difficult. Later, with the intensified efforts of the engineers stationed in the section, day and night, all have now been built above the water surface, and it will take only about a month to complete. However, the three major bridge projects in the northern section, including the Lu, Mi, and Lei Rivers, except for the Mi River, which has been completed in the season, continuous rain has caused the Xiang River to rise from time to time, resulting in several bridge piers being built deeper in the riverbed being repeatedly suspended and often obstructed. The two bridges will be opened to traffic in the next month and a half, without waiting for all the steel beams to be erected, so that the rail connection of the entire line can be realized ahead of schedule. As for the track-laying work, the northern section has already arrived at Hengshan from Zhuzhou and is continuing to extend southward. It is estimated that it will be laid to Hengyang in about two months. South of Hengyang, it is already possible to reach Loufengdu in the county of Chenzhou. It will soon reach Chenzhou Station. The remaining 60-kilometer section of solid rock roadbed in the Hepu line from Chenzhou to Pingshi in Guangdong has taken shape, and the mountain tunnels have also been completed. From now on, it will not be affected by weather or human affairs, so the connection between the north and south ends should not be far away.

Fuzhou Commercial Crisis

The Scope of Loans from the Three Banks is Still Small; Recovery of Southeast Business is Feared to be Difficult; A First-Class Silk Store Suddenly Declares Bankruptcy

Fuzhou Correspondence: The business community in this city previously requested the establishment of a commercial public treasury and the issuance of circulating notes due to tight money during the year-end settlement period. The Ministry of Finance rejected the request because it conflicted with the decree prohibiting the issuance of private currency and ordered the Fuzhou Central, China, and Transportation Banks to allocate one million yuan to rescue the financial market. After Provincial Chairman Chen Yi returned to Fujian, he specifically summoned the heads of the Central, China, and Transportation Banks to the government to discuss rescue measures and decided that the provincial government, county chamber of commerce, and the three banks would each elect three people to form a financial maintenance committee to handle loan matters. Any merchant in need of funds can submit real estate and request the committee to assess the price and borrow funds from the bank. However, although the nominal value is 100% of the property value, only 50% can be borrowed. In reality, real estate can only be assessed at 80% of the lowest market price, and the maximum loan amount can only be pledged at about 40%. Therefore, if they rely entirely on mortgaging property to borrow money for turnover, it will still not solve the problem, and it can only be used as a partial aid. Merchants are extremely eager for the committee to be established as soon as possible because they are in urgent need of funds. It is now reported that the provincial government intends to appoint Xu Fu, Chen Ticheng, and Lin Zhiyuan, the chamber of commerce intends to appoint Luo Mianhou, Chen Peikun, and Hong Fasui, and the bank will be represented by the heads of the three banks. However, after the committee is established, another evaluation committee must be formed to specialize in assessing house prices, so it will not be possible to start operating until after the fifteenth day of the twelfth lunar month at the earliest.

After the Southeast Bank suspended business, the provincial government organized a reorganization committee to liquidate creditors and debtors. The original plan was to resume business or reorganize, but more than a month has passed, but only more than 300,000 yuan of debts owed by people have been recovered, and most of the debts owed were embezzled by the bank's directors, managers, and important staff to operate other private businesses, which cannot be recovered. Calculating the currently received funds and the funds transferred from real estate mortgages, it is only enough to pay 50% of the amount of the issued banknotes. As for the original plan to resume business or reorganize, it is feared that it will be difficult to realize.

The situation in the commercial market is becoming more and more difficult as the settlement period approaches. Among them, the silk and cloth gangs of Jiangsu and Guangdong are the most exhausted. Because the shops of these two gangs, due to the depression of the market, purchased large quantities of goods on credit between summer and autumn and held large-scale sales to maintain their appearance. Now that the end of the year has arrived, they have no money to pay their debts and are all on the verge of collapse. Yesterday, Fan Yonghua Fine Cloth Store in Taijiang declared bankruptcy first, owing more than 20,000 yuan. It is found that Taijiang Fan is the concentrated area of silk and cloth stores in Jiangsu and Guangdong in this city. It is extremely prosperous on the surface on weekdays, but extremely empty inside. Yonghua is a first-class store in the area, only owing 20,000 yuan, and it has declared bankruptcy. Then other companies will inevitably be affected by it. Therefore, in these 20 or so days, it is a time of major commercial crisis in Fuzhou.

Double Year-End Approaches; Jiangxi Obtains Loans from Three Banks

All Counties and Towns Unanimously Request Relief; Small and Medium-Sized Merchants Request Permission to Mortgage Furniture

Nanchang Correspondence: Jiangxi's economy this year is depleted, and the market is depressed, which is unprecedented. At this time of the new and old year-end, everything is felt to be more difficult and tense. Finance Commissioner Wu Riqian went to Beijing and Shanghai a few days ago to contact Finance Minister Kong for this reason, requesting that the Central, China, and Transportation Banks lend two million yuan to the Jiangxi Provincial Yumin Bank to handle loan procedures to curb bankruptcy. The general method is: the types of loans are divided into two parts: (A) Goods mortgage: the borrower shall mortgage the Yumin Bank according to the normal goods mortgage procedures, and then the Yumin Bank shall re-mortgage the three banks. This item of goods is limited to those that can be actually transferred and occupied. (B) If the goods cannot be transferred and occupied temporarily, the borrower shall submit real estate as a second guarantee and specify the type, quantity, and value of the goods, issue notes, and mortgage them to the Yumin Bank, and then the Yumin Bank shall re-discount them to the three banks. The former loan, A accounts for 70%, and B accounts for 30%. Yumin's re-mortgage and re-discount to the three banks must be approved by the three banks first. The loan period is limited to four months. If the loan cannot be repaid on schedule, the provincial government is requested to give special flexible regulations for the borrower and guarantor and allow administrative sanctions. As for the loan review committee, it has been established and started lending on the 24th. However, after the news that the Finance Department borrowed two million yuan spread, all 83 county and town chambers of commerce petitioned to universally lend money for relief. The Finance Department rejected the petitions, saying that it could only provide relief to the market and had no power to universalize it. It is reported that the porcelain industry in Jingdezhen will be allocated another 200,000 yuan by the provincial government and the National Economic Commission to provide relief to this world-famous special product. However, in this city, only those with property can get loans, and small and medium-sized merchants cannot avoid being excluded. Therefore, rescue associations were organized by various industries to request loans with shop bottoms, docks, and furniture, and repeatedly petitioned Commissioner Wu. Wu said that the three banks could not agree to this type of mortgage. The commercial rescue association believed that small and medium-sized merchants would have no way to go. Furthermore, the Shanghai Commercial & Savings Bank absorbed two or three million yuan of small deposits from the lower classes in Jiangxi, which should be released in Jiangxi and should not be transferred to Shanghai. It also petitioned the Finance Department to forward it to the Shanghai Bank to handle loans for small and medium-sized industrial and commercial enterprises. Therefore, Cheng Shunyuan, the manager of the Jiangxi branch of the bank, has gone to Shanghai to ask the head office for instructions.

Later, the ward chief Ye Xingquan reported it to the local court. Prosecutor Shen took the Wang coroner and others to examine the body. It was also found that the man had the words "Lin Jinsheng" and an anchor tattooed on his left hand. After the examination was completed, because there were no family members, the ward chief prepared a coffin to collect the body and waited for the arrest of the murderer.

The county government ordered him to be detained for verification.

Changshu: Water Police Officer Commits Suicide Due to Illness and Despair

Wang Yunsheng, a soldier of the Second Detachment of the Fourth Water Police Team stationed in Hupu, had enlisted for many years. He was usually healthy, but unexpectedly, he suddenly suffered from lung disease in the past two months, coughing non-stop and unable to sleep at night. Because he was trapped in economic difficulties, he could not afford medical treatment and had a motive for despair. Fortunately, he was persuaded by his friends and did not succeed. Unexpectedly, his illness became more and more severe recently. On the night before, taking advantage of the unpreparedness of others, he loaded a Mauser rifle with live ammunition, tied a thin rope to the trigger, and moved his foot to pull it. With a bang, the bullet entered his heart and exited from his back. When his colleagues heard the sound and got up to look, they saw Wang Yunsheng lying in a pool of blood and unable to be saved. The county was notified immediately, and an official was sent to the countryside on the 4th to examine the body. Wang was 29 years old and from Cixi, Zhejiang.

Yangzhou: Jiuxing Bridge Collapses for Dozens of Feet

The Jiuxing Bridge (Jiangbei) pier of the Puji Ferry collapsed at about 3:00 a.m. on the 4th, with a length of more than ten feet and a width of six or seven feet collapsing on the river bank. Residents were all in a dream, only hearing a strange sound. They only realized it at dawn. Fortunately, no one was injured. The ferries that opened from Siyuan Canal that morning all went straight to Zhenjiang and returned to Guazhou to disembark passengers. The Jiangbei passengers under Jiuxing Bridge disembarked at Guazhou and changed to short shifts to Yangzhou.

Hangzhou: Mastermind of Robbery and Kidnapping Escorted to Hangzhou

Huang Xikun, a Chinese bank clerk in Hangzhou, was escorting remittances to No. 46 Shangcangqiao Zhijie on April 27th of this year when he was murdered by bandits and robbed of more than 6,000 yuan in cash. The case occurred eight months ago. After a thorough investigation by the Hangzhou Public Security Bureau, a clue was obtained. On December 18th, Jiang Mingxia was captured at the Meichi station on the Zhejiang-Jiangxi Railway. He confessed that he had committed the robbery together with Xie Qifeng, Lu Xingxuan, and others. Later, detectives were sent to Changxing to capture Lu Xingxuan. He also confessed that he and Xie committed the crime of kidnapping the four-year-old young son of Sun Xiyun, the owner of the Jianggan Qianzhi Sugar Store, demanding a ransom of seven years, tearing up the ticket, and shooting the driver when raising the ticket. Moreover, Xie was the mastermind in both cases. Xie fled to Shaanxi immediately after the incident. The Xi'an Public Security Bureau was notified by telegram to arrest him in the Shandong apartment and send someone to escort him. He arrived in Hangzhou last night and was sent to the Public Security Bureau. Xie tried to commit suicide repeatedly on the way, so he was taken care of properly. The bandits were all college students. Jiang was a student at the Shanghai Business and Political College, Xie was a student at the Southeast Medical College, and Xie was a student at the Tongji Medical College. The three were all close relatives. Lu's father had served as the magistrate of Haining County and the director of the Stamp Tobacco and Alcohol Bureau.

Pinghu: Tongyixing Rice Store Robbed

Tongyixing Rice Store, outside the West Gate of Zhapu, has been open for many years and has a lot of savings. At midnight at the end of last month, seven bandits suddenly broke in through the back door with box guns and sharp blades, scaring the store owner Jiang Wenbin and his son into silence. They robbed a lot of cash, jewelry, clothes, and bedding. The bandits were still not satisfied. They took off the shoes and socks of Xiao Dongjiang Zirong and burned his toes with Western candle fire. Zirong shouted in pain, and the bandits, fearing it would be unfavorable, fired two shots and left. The store had been robbed not long ago. Having suffered two losses, they were unwilling to accept it. They opened a loss list and submitted it to the Second Public Security Bureau, begging for investigation.

Xiaoshan: Meat Shops in the Urban Area Go on Strike

Due to the county government's increase of two cents of education surcharge per pig, all the fresh meat shop operators in the urban area opposed it. While they were holding a meeting at the Chamber of Commerce on the 31st, the county government sent police to summon the operators to the county. Since it could not be resolved, the two directors, Chen and Fu, were detained, causing all 15 meat shops in the urban area to go on strike from New Year's Day. As of noon on the 3rd, the county government had not released the directors, so the fresh meat shops in the urban area had not opened. On the afternoon of the 3rd, all the meat shop operators, in addition to sending telegrams to the provincial government's finance and education departments, also petitioned the Party Headquarters, saying that the county magistrate abused his power, detained the directors, and forced the closure of the market, and asked for relief.

Education Broadcasting Special Issue

National Language Course Lecture: How to Write (Continued)

— Ye Shaojun, Editor of Kaiming Bookstore

In the past, people who learned to write articles paid attention to reciting scriptures, often saying that as long as they read dozens of articles thoroughly, they would naturally be able to write. This sounds mysterious, but the principle is very common. It turns out that it means cultivating language habits. Literary Chinese is different from spoken language. Not only are the words used different, but also a part of the sentence structure is very different. To learn to write literary Chinese that is different from spoken language, there is no other way than to learn this special language habit, and recitation is a cultivation to learn this special language habit. Therefore, putting aside other aspects and only talking about the method of learning to write articles from recitation in the past, that is correct. If you want to learn to write literary Chinese now, I think you should also start with reciting literary Chinese. However, I don't think you really need to write literary Chinese. Saying that the vernacular is shallow and the literary Chinese is deep, and that learning the vernacular first and then the literary Chinese is a gradual process from shallow to deep, this statement is really unreasonable. The shallowness and depth of an article should be determined by the content and technology, not by whether the style is vernacular or literary Chinese. If the content is good and the expression technology is also good, even if it is the vernacular, it is also deep. If the content is bad and the expression technology is also bad, even if it is the literary Chinese, it is also shallow. Moreover, since we are modern people, to express our thoughts and feelings, we naturally use modern language in speech, and naturally use the vernacular written according to the spoken language in writing. Being able to write the vernacular, we already have the most convenient tool, so why should we go to learn a kind of impractical literary Chinese? If it is said that in college entrance examinations or other examinations, there is often a bracket added under the Chinese language topic, and the four words "limited to literary Chinese" are written in the bracket, so you have to prepare in advance. This is really because the people in charge of the examination are too ignorant. We hope that they will gradually become enlightened and no longer do this kind of deliberately making things difficult for people without any practical significance in the near future. But before this fact has completely disappeared, you have to spare some time to learn to write literary Chinese for the sake of entering school and passing other examinations.

The above said a lot of words, nothing more than to explain that the most important thing to write fluent articles is to cultivate our language habits. Because we believe that articles are records of language, and the two are originally the same thing, but we have to go further. When we write articles, we cannot fail to know the differences between articles and language. As mentioned earlier, when speaking, there are facial expressions and body postures as help, but articles do not have this help, which is the difference. Knowing that there is this layer, we have to pay special attention when writing articles, how to write appropriately, so that we can make people understand without relying on this help. Are there only this layer of differences? Below, we will say some more. For example, when two people chat, they often talk from the south to the north, and the ending can be completely unrelated to the beginning. Even when discussing a problem or discussing a matter, sometimes a digression is added in the middle, like vines crawling away, crawling completely away from the topic, until one person realizes it and says, "Let's talk about serious business," then it is cut off with a knife and returns to the topic again. Articles cannot be like this. Most articles are prepared for people to read, and a small part is left for themselves to check in the future. Every article has a center. Without a center, there is no need to write, so when writing, only words related to the center should be written in, and they should be arranged very properly so that the center is completely revealed. As for those unconstrained random words, like vines crawling away, should be eliminated completely, so that they do not waste our writing. For example, when narrating a thing in language, it is often verbose and does not omit small things. If you convey a conversation, you have to narrate it as it is, one is one, two is two, what A said, what B said, what A said again, what B said again. Articles cannot be like this. Articles strive for convenience for both writing and reading, so they should pay attention to economy. If you leave out all the important words, an article does not reveal any center, which is not economical. You must write all the important things in. In addition, there is no verbose word. It is just like being good at using money. You should never save money where you should not save money, and you should never spend a penny where you should not spend money. This is enough to be called economy. Under this condition, narrating a thing has to pay attention to the method of detail and brevity. The narrative of the process of the thing is not of the same amount. You must teach people to understand the detailed parts and do not hesitate to spend a lot of writing. The parts that do not need to be taught to people in detail can be passed over in one stroke. If you record people's conversations, you have to pay attention to the effort of selection. You do not make a complete record of people's language. Only those that can show their thoughts, insights, temperament, etc. are allowed to be selected, otherwise, it is okay to leave them out. For example, when we speak, we often use local dialects and the special tones of the local language. Articles are not like this. Articles have to look at the reader's origin. If an article is prepared for people from all over the world to read, it should use the vocabulary and tones that are common in various places. The vocabulary and tones that are only common in the local area must be completely eliminated, so that the disadvantages of barriers can be avoided. The above are all the differences between articles and language. Knowing these layers also knows the outline of writing technology. Knowledge gradually becomes a habit, so writing has the convenience of recording language without the disadvantage of rigidly recording language.

Now come to an end. How to write? The most important thing is to cultivate our language habits. If the language habits are good, the articles written will be fluent. Secondly, it is important to distinguish the differences between articles and language. If you understand the distinction, you can know and do, and the articles you write will not only be fluent, but also complete and beyond reproach. (End)
