President Jiang Arrived in Shanghai Yesterday, Comforted Mr. Wang, and Immediately Returned to Nanjing

Met with Mayor Wu and Others to Inquire about Shanghai's Municipal Administration, Visited Duan Qirui and Huang Fu, and Paid Homage to the Song Mausoleum

President Jiang of the Executive Yuan, accompanied by Secretary Mr. Wang Rizhang, took the night train from Nanjing to Shanghai at 11:00 p.m. the night before. He arrived at the station at 6:49 a.m. yesterday morning. Shanghai Mayor Wu Tiecheng, Director Yang Hu of the Municipal Security Bureau, the son of Mr. Kong Xiangxi, Vice President of the Executive Yuan and Minister of Finance, and Secretary Wang Zhinan of the Municipal Security Bureau all went to Zhenru Station to welcome him. President Jiang was wearing a blue robe and black jacket, and a cloak on the outside. He looked energetic. After getting off the train, he went straight to his private residence on Jia'er Yeai Road to rest. The surrounding area of Zhenru Station and Zhongshan Road were all guarded by the security team, and the security was very strict.

Comforting Mr. Wang

President Jiang arrived at his private residence on Jia'er Yeai Road at 7:25 a.m. He met with Mayor Wu and Director Yang and inquired about Shanghai's municipal administration and public security. Then at 9:40 a.m., he went to Anhe Temple Road to visit the Chairman of the Central Political Committee, and expressed his condolences. He also hoped that after Mr. Wang recovered, he would return to Nanjing as soon as possible to share the heavy responsibility. They talked for half an hour before leaving.

Visiting Mr. Huang and Duan President Jiang went straight to Qiqi Road to meet with Mr. Huang Yingbai, the former Minister of Interior, after leaving Mr. Wang's residence. They had some discussions. He left at 10:45 a.m. and then went to Avenue Joffre to meet with Mr. Duan Qirui. He did not leave until 11:25 a.m. and returned to his private residence on Jia'er Yeai Road to rest.

Paying Homage to the Song Mausoleum Later, President Jiang, accompanied by his wife, Ms. Song Meiling, went to the International Cemetery on Hongqiao Road at 11:40 a.m. to pay homage to the tomb of the Song Madame and presented flowers to pay respect. Then he went to Seymour Road and planned to visit Mr. Xu Chongzhi, Vice President of the Control Yuan, but Mr. Xu had already gone to Nanjing and could not meet him. Then he went to Mr. Kong's old residence to rest for a while. At 12:35 p.m., he was invited by Mr. and Mrs. Kong to have lunch at Mr. Kong's residence on West Avenue de Ames. Mr. Song Ziwen and Mr. Yu Qiaqing, standing members of the National Economic Commission, visited President Jiang one after another yesterday afternoon, but they did not meet him because President Jiang was out.

Flying to Nanjing on the Same Day President Jiang left Mr. Kong's residence at 3:30 p.m. and visited Mr. Song Ziwen, standing member of the National Economic Commission. After a brief chat, he left and went straight to Hongqiao Airport. At 3:45 p.m., he took a Savoia plane back to Nanjing. Those who went to the airport to see him off included Mrs. Jiang Song Meiling, Mr. and Mrs. Kong Xiangxi, Mr. Song Ziwen, Ziliang, Zian and other brothers, as well as Mr. Wu Tiecheng, Yang Hu, Wei Daoming, Wang Zhinan, and others. Only Secretary Wang Rizhang and several guards accompanied President Jiang to Nanjing.

County Public Security Bureau - Respectfully Informing Newly Reformed Opium Smokers

The Shanghai County Public Security Bureau, starting from February 1st of this year, has designated this as the period for the overall inspection against opium smoking. To ensure opium smokers understand the significance of this, they have specifically issued a respectful announcement to newly reformed opium smokers, hoping they will awaken as soon as possible.

Now, we present the original text below, so everyone should know: Our China is now in the most critical and difficult period. The biggest cause of this situation is the scourge of opium. Therefore, the government has made a resolute decision to ban opium and will absolutely no longer be lenient. The formulated anti-opium laws are very strict and impactful. Opium smokers who privately smoke without a license or relapse after quitting will face severe penalties, possibly even the death penalty. Originally, a person who smokes opium will harm their health, shorten their lifespan, and lose their wealth, becoming more ghost than human. Good relatives and friends will look down on them, and close parents and spouses will ignore them. Even if the government did not ban it, what pleasure is there in smoking opium? Moreover, under such a tightly woven net of laws, why bother to bring trouble upon oneself? Since this province effectively implemented the opium ban last year, opium cessation licenses have now been issued for the third term. Many determined opium smokers have completely quit, escaped the suffering of being blacklisted, and returned to being honest citizens. This is indeed a good phenomenon. However, there are still many opium smokers who, for various reasons during the general registration, did not register with the government to obtain a license to quit opium. The government is also well aware of this. Now, out of consideration for these unfortunate unregistered opium smokers, it is stipulated that from January 1st to the end of the month of the 25th year of the Republic, there will be a registration period for newly reformed opium smokers. During this period, being able to resolve to quit is the best opportunity. If, due to illness or old age, one cannot quit temporarily, paying the third-term license fee to the government will exempt one from the penalty for unlicensed private smoking. If one insists on remaining unenlightened, once the deadline expires, the overall inspection will be implemented starting from February 1st. Our public security organs, in order to fulfill the responsibility of strictly enforcing the law, will honestly and without being polite, implement arrests and will absolutely not be lenient. We hope that opium smokers who have not obtained a license to quit smoking will pay attention quickly and take advantage of this opportunity for newly reformed registration to turn back to the right path!

Postal Savings Bureau Announcement - National Simple Life Insurance

Other insurance companies are prohibited from operating it.

The Postal Savings and Remittance Bureau issued an announcement yesterday stating, "Upon examination of Article 1 of the Simple Life Insurance Law, it is stated that simple life insurance is a national enterprise under the jurisdiction of the Ministry of Communications, and other insurance operators are prohibited from operating it. Also, Article 1 of the Simple Life Insurance Regulations states that all life insurance policies from fifty to five hundred yuan, whether for individuals or groups, fall within the scope of simple life insurance, and so on. The aforementioned Simple Life Insurance Law and Regulations have been promulgated by the National Government and came into effect on December 1st of the 24th year of the Republic. From the date of implementation, all life insurance policies within the scope of simple life insurance, whether already in operation or not, should be handled by this bureau in accordance with laws and regulations. This announcement is hereby made."

The Xinsheng News Agency reports that the Ministry of Railways, in order to construct the Nanping section of the Zhejiang-Jiangxi Railway, is issuing the second phase of railway construction bonds for the 25th year of the Republic for 27 million yuan. It has been approved by the Executive Yuan to mortgage 16 million yuan to a banking syndicate composed of the Bank of China and other banks, as well as the German Otto Wolff Iron Factory. An agreement in principle has been reached, and a contract will soon be negotiated. Details are as follows:

Continuing to Issue Bonds

The Hangzhou to Yushan section of the Zhejiang-Jiangxi Railway,

Approved by the Executive Yuan

350 kilometers long, has long been completed and open to traffic. Now, it is planned to replace the 35-pound light rails with 63-pound heavy rails.

The Yushan to Nanchang section, 300 kilometers long, has now been completed and officially opened to traffic, scheduled for January 15th.

The Nanchang to Pingxiang section, 290 kilometers long, has been surveyed and will soon begin construction.

As for the funding, it has been decided that the Ministry of Railways will issue the second phase of railway construction bonds for 27 million yuan. Minister Zhang Gongquan has drafted the bond regulations and the repayment and interest schedule, which were approved by the Executive Yuan's regular meeting on the 31st of last month.

Negotiating the Mortgage

Regarding the mortgage of the second phase of railway

Agreement in Principle Reached

construction bonds, the chairman of the Zhejiang-Jiangxi Railway, Zhu Yangfu (now the Minister of the Ministry of Railways), and the representative of the banking syndicate composed of the Bank of China and other banks, as well as the Shanghai representative of the German Otto Wolff Iron Factory, have been in contact and have reached an agreement in principle. The face value of the bonds is 27 million yuan, with 8 million yuan mortgaged to the banking syndicate in cash and 8 million yuan mortgaged to the iron factory in materials. These bonds will be kept by the banking syndicate composed of the Bank of China and other banks. All procedures are the same as the mortgage procedures for the first phase of railway bonds and the Yushan-Pingxiang Railway bonds.

Soon to Negotiate

The Ministry of Railways has, since August of last year,

Mortgage Contract

allocated 250,000 yuan from the surplus each month as a fund for issuing the second phase of bonds. At the same time, he will meet with Chen Bilin of the Shanghai office of the Zhejiang-Jiangxi Railway Materials Purchasing Committee and the Shanghai representative of the iron factory to discuss the prices of materials. After the contract is signed, a telegram will be sent to Germany to transport the materials to China for use.

Shanghai County - Yesterday's Rice Stem Borer Eradication Meeting - Resolved to Guide Farmers to Dig Up and Burn Rice Roots

The Shanghai County Rice Stem Borer Eradication Committee held its second meeting at 2:00 PM yesterday in the county government conference room. Committee members Zhang Yi, Fu Dianying, Zhang Jingye, Huang Meixian, Jin Zuobin, Ding Hongzhang, Xu Yuyin, Ye Zhendong, etc. were present. The meeting was chaired by Ye Zhendong and recorded by Li Tongrui. After the meeting began as scheduled, the chairman first reported that the Construction Bureau had instructed that the county should still guide farmers to collect and burn rice roots exposed above the soil. The case was handled accordingly and continued to discuss how to handle it. It was resolved that the county government should order the Public Security Bureau and various district offices to, together with the people's education halls, beat gongs to advise farmers to dig up and burn all rice roots exposed above the soil within half a month of receiving the notice. Then, the township and baojia chiefs should investigate and report to the district offices under their jurisdiction, which in turn should report to the county government to request the Construction Bureau to send personnel to inspect.

Japan and Germany Order Chinese Cotton - National Cotton Exports Increase Sharply - Japanese Merchants Purchase 160,000 Dan in Nantong, German Merchants Purchase 5,000 Dan, Still in Initial Stages

The Shenshi News Agency reports that after the National Economic Commission's Cotton Industry Control Association actively improved cotton production in various parts of China, the quality has been improving day by day. The cotton produced in the two major cotton-producing areas, such as Nantong in Jiangsu and Shaanxi, is of excellent quality and is very popular among foreign merchants. Since October of last year, cotton exports have been huge, with the largest amount being exported to Japan. In three months, Japanese merchants have ordered 160,000 dan of Chinese cotton, a rare surge in recent years. According to sources in the cotton industry, Germany has also recently ordered 5,000 dan of cotton from Nantong, China. In the past, Germany purchased all the cotton it needed from the United States. Purchasing from China is still in its initial stages. This year, due to curbing the large-scale import of American cotton and the impact of the Italian-Abyssinian War, Indian cotton exports to Germany have sharply decreased, so it has had to purchase from China. In the future, it is expected that exports of domestic cotton to Germany will continue to increase.

Issuance Reserve Management Committee - Inspecting the Legal Tender Reserves of the Three Banks - Reporting to the Ministry of Finance for Record and Announcing Monthly

The Xinsheng News Agency reports that after the Ministry of Finance stipulated on November 4th of last year that the banknotes of the Central Bank of China, Bank of China, and Bank of Communications would be legal tender, it also established an Issuance Reserve Management Committee to inspect the issuance amounts and reserves of the Zhejiang Industrial Bank, China Industrial Bank, China Agricultural and Industrial Bank, Kenye Bank, Siming Bank, and Commercial, Agricultural, and Industrial Banks. The inspection rules have now been promulgated by the Ministry, and the Issuance Reserve Management Committee has followed the rules to ensure that the issuance of legal tender is fully backed by reserves in accordance with the issuance amount. Cash reserves account for 60%, consisting of gold, silver, or foreign exchange. Security reserves account for 40%, consisting of valuable securities issued or guaranteed by the National Government and other assets or short-term commercial paper deemed reliable by the Ministry of Finance. Committee members such as Ye Zhuotang are dispatched monthly to inspect the Central Bank of China, Bank of China, and Bank of Communications once to demonstrate trustworthiness. In addition to reporting to the Ministry of Finance, it is also announced publicly. As for Tianjin, Hankou, and other places, the legal tender reserves of those with branch committees of the Issuance Reserve Management Committee are inspected by the branch committees.

Machine Factory Joint Association Notifies Factories - Automatic Inspection of Fire Hazards

Printed Automatic Inspection Method for Factory Safety Equipment

Distributed to Each Factory for Preparation to Eliminate Disasters

The Shanghai Machine-Made National Products Factory Joint Association believes that the occurrence of fire hazards has a significant impact on life and property. Moreover, factories have vast areas, strong capital, and many workers. The concern for life and property is more than dozens or hundreds of times greater. Therefore, to eliminate disasters, continuous inspection is essential. Therefore, it has specifically printed the Automatic Inspection Method for Factory Safety Equipment and notified each factory for reference and implementation. The following is an excerpt:

Notice to Each Factory

The Shanghai Machine-Made National Products Factory Joint Association notifies each factory: Greetings. In the past, Confucius saw a golden statue in the Zhou Temple with its mouth sealed three times and inscribed on its back: "The ancient person who was careful with words." The saying goes, "One word can build a nation, and one word can destroy a nation." It can be seen that disaster comes from the mouth, and its impact is so great. For example, if a fire occurs now, life and property will be reduced to ashes. Those who have fire insurance can, after cleaning up the ashes, rely on the insurance company's compensation to reorganize. However, if the cause of the fire, after investigation, is proven to contradict the clauses attached to the issued policy, the insurance company may refuse its responsibility, pay only a part, or even not pay at all. Then, the factory that has the fire suffers greatly. Therefore, employees should not talk nonsense or speculate about the cause of the fire and should know to be cautious. It should also be known that the occurrence of unfortunate events is not limited to fire. Any event should imitate the golden statue's three seals on its mouth. Now, because the attached Automatic Inspection Method for Factory Safety Equipment is included, it is specially sent to you. We hope you pay attention to it. Sincerely, we wish you public peace.

Automatic Inspection

Automatic Inspection Method for Factory Safety Equipment

In factories, it is often necessary to accumulate fuel and store raw materials, which often causes fire. The most likely sources of fire in factories are:

Boilers, fuel rooms, steam pipes, machine friction

Air engines, generators, electrical transformers, electricity

Gas pipes, gas stoves, etc.

Kerosene, gasoline

Candles, lighters, and chemical drugs

Coal piles

Alcohol, wood, paper, etc.

Marsh gas in ditches, naturally ignited objects. Because there are flammable items, and even naturally flammable items, the spread of the fire can quickly turn into a prairie fire. If there are raw materials to help it burn, once a fire starts, it is beyond remedy. If each factory does not have sufficient fire prevention equipment and training on a daily basis, it is inevitable that a tragedy will occur, and even lives will be affected. The intensity of the harm is unimaginable. We hope that those who are in factories do not take it lightly. The effective methods of defense are as follows:

(A) Architectural Equipment and Inspection

Factories are best built with steel-reinforced concrete.

Material and fuel storage areas should be built with cavity walls or fire-resistant bricks.

If wood is used in places with a slight possibility of ignition, the wood should be treated with a chemical solution to make it difficult to ignite. Fire-resistant solutions can be purchased from the Pingan Industrial Factory.

Important offices should not be close to boiler rooms or fuel rooms.

Factories should adopt low-rise buildings and should not be too high.

The roof should not be made of flammable materials.

Install more emergency exits and fire escape ladders (are there piles of objects at the entrance and ladder side?)

Install fire hydrants (B) Non-Architectural Equipment and Inspection

Automatic fire extinguishing devices (installed?)

Fire alarm (installed?)

Fire extinguishers (purchased?)

Fire buckets and sand buckets (installed?)

Ladders, iron hooks, etc. (installed?)

Other rescue equipment

(C) Management Equipment and Inspection

Organize a fire brigade. The number of team members depends on the size of the factory. Set up a fire chief to lead them. If the fire brigade is large, several team leaders can be established, led by the general captain. (For factory fire drills, please refer to my book "Fire Prevention Method" (General Sales by Life Bookstore)

Training of fire brigade members

Training of general workers

Establish close contact with the police authorities

Workers are not allowed to smoke while working, and when smoking during breaks, they must do so in the smoking room or in an open area. (Strictly punish those who throw cigarette butts and sparks)

The general captain should always observe the workers' laziness and caution. Those who contribute to the fire brigade should be rewarded, and those who are negligent should be punished.

A separate annual fire prevention expense should be set up in the accounting book.

The above are just general situations. Factories can choose to adopt them according to their different environments. We hope that industrialists can pay attention to this, and unfortunate events can be reduced, and the investment of capitalists and the lives of workers can be further protected.

General Employees and Passengers - Prohibited from Embarking and Disembarking at Wusong Port

Jianghai Customs Imposes Prohibition - Shipping Industry Unanimously Opposes

Shanghai's pilotage is divided into two types: one is for ocean-going ships, which are guided to Shanghai from the Tongsha sea area. The pilotage rights have long been controlled by foreigners. Although Chinese have striven for it in recent years, and with the establishment of the Jiang Gong Association, most of the pilots for river vessels are Chinese. Since last year, after the Jianghai Customs acquired the pilotage rights for this route, the Yangtze River pilotage must also be controlled by the Customs. Chinese who hold this position must pass the Customs examination and be deemed qualified before being appointed. The power of selection rests with foreign advisors. The situation is inverted, which hinders national prestige. After the Customs acquired the Yangtze River pilotage rights, it notified each shipping company that the hiring of pilots for Chinese ships must be requested from the Customs, and they are not allowed to hire on their own as they did in the past. Also, fearing that each shipping company would resist or hire privately, the Customs authorities, in order to achieve the goal of unified assignment by the Customs, imposed a prohibition: all Chinese merchant ships passing through Wusong Port are prohibited from freely embarking and disembarking, regardless of whether they are passengers or crew members. Since the promulgation of this prohibition, passengers on river vessels directly traveling to and from the river are no longer allowed to disembark at Wusong. They can only go to Shanghai and then to Wusong, and the loss and pain are still minor. Those who take ships from other ports directly to the Yangtze River can, as usual, land. If crew members take the opportunity to return to Shanghai or passengers take the opportunity to visit Shanghai, now because of the Customs prohibition, all are prohibited from embarking and disembarking. In recent days, crew members and passengers on Chinese merchant ships have been unduly prohibited, and the number of those who cannot go to Shanghai is more than several hundred. This is not a national prohibition. Since its implementation, Wusong Port has been greatly affected, and Chinese merchant ships no longer dock. Only some foreign merchant ships remain. In recent days, the unexpected losses suffered by each Chinese merchant ship due to this semi-blockade have aroused the anger of all shipping companies. The crew members and passengers on each ship are even more heartbroken after being prohibited from embarking and disembarking at Wusong Port by the Customs. Now, they have jointly named and telegraphed the central government, expressing unanimous protest. The crew member organizations have also submitted reports to the Ministry of Finance and the Ministry of Communications, demanding the revocation of this informal Customs prohibition that hinders land and sea transportation, and the anti-protest telegrams have all been sent.

Silver and Money Industries - Preparing Treasury Loans Suddenly Busy

The purpose is to alleviate financial difficulties and ensure a stable passage through the difficulties.

The Bank Preparation Committee was established on March 15th of the 21st year of the Republic and has achieved considerable results. All member banks will (A) Real estate within the Shanghai International Settlement and the French Concession, (B) Goods that can be immediately converted into cash, (C) Stocks or bonds with value on the London or New York market, and deposits abroad, (D) Cash coins or redeemable gold coins or cash notes, (E) Other properties not within the scope of the previous four items, but permitted by the Executive Committee, are considered prepared assets, and after evaluation by the Evaluation Committee at 70% of the estimated value, public notes are issued at 50% and treasury certificates at 50%. When member banks need cash, they can borrow cash from the committee using public notes. The period is set to one day. The committee publishes the daily public note loan interest and public note discount rate. The treasury can be used as a guarantee reserve for savings deposits and the issuance of exchange notes.

The Money Industry Joint Reserve Treasury was established on October 1st of the 21st year of the Republic and has achieved considerable results. All member money houses will (A) Bills of lading for goods that can be immediately converted into cash, (B) Real estate with estimated value within the city, (C) Cash coins or cash notes, (D) Actual large notes or silver dollars as prepared assets. The treasury handles deposit and overdraft matters for various firms in the same industry in accordance with Article 11 of the regulations. The overdraft period is one day, and the minimum interest rate is 20 per thousand per week. It accepts notes from the same industry submitted to the bank by 3:00 PM. Overdue amounts will be accounted for the next day. The deadline for money house checks is 5:00 PM. (Xinsheng News Agency)

End of Student Domestic Products Year: Statistics on Educational Imports

Total Value Exceeds 16 Million National Currency Units; Scientific Instruments Account for the Largest Share of Imports

The Student Domestic Products Year has come to an end. The import figures for educational supplies during the past year should be of concern to all sectors. A New News Agency reporter has made a special inquiry to the Statistics Office of the International Trade Bureau and recorded the details as follows:

Total Import Value

Last year was the Student Domestic Products Year. During this year, the total import value of educational supplies was 7,194,000+ gold units, equivalent to 16,070,000+ national currency units. This is a slight decrease compared to the 7,753,426 gold units of the same period last year, but the decrease is minimal, only about 7%. This shows that the efforts of the academic community in promoting domestic products seem to be not yet thorough. It is hoped that all sectors of education will continue to work hard in the future.

Scientific Instruments

The largest import value of educational supplies is for scientific instruments, valued at 2,897,000+ gold units. Next are books and sheet music, valued at 2,766,000+ units. Followed by printing ink and ink, etc., valued at 858,000+ units. Sports and other games equipment are valued at 635,000+ gold units. Maps and drawings are also valued at 36,000+ gold units. Except for gasoline ink and drawings, the import values this year have decreased compared to the same period last year. The largest decrease is in books and sheet music, which decreased by about 16%. Although other commodities have declined, the decrease is very small.

Country of Origin

As for the source of imports and educational supplies, according to the survey by the Statistics Office of the International Trade Bureau, three-fifths of the imported scientific instruments are of German origin, followed by the United States. Japanese and British goods also have a considerable share. As for books and sheet music, more are imported from the United States than from Europe. Printing ink and ink mostly come from the United Kingdom. In addition, many are also shipped from Japan and Germany.

Zhejiang-Jiangxi Railway Extends Special Rate for Coarse Paper Transport for One Year

The directorate of the two railways, the Thailand Railway Ministry, instructed: "According to the Zhejiang-Jiangxi Railway Bureau's report, the special rate for the four-way joint transport of coarse paper, which the railway has agreed on with Jinghu, Huhangyong, and Jinpu, was previously approved to be implemented on a trial basis for six months from July 1, 1935. From July 1 of this year to the end of November, a total of more than 2,190 tons were exported during the special rate period. Although the quantity is not large, it is sufficient to prove that the special rate method still has absorption capacity compared to the previous rare exports. It is also found that the export period of the coarse paper is in the Qingming and Winter Solstice seasons, and the Winter Solstice season is especially high. It is proposed to approve the extension of the handling period for one year to attract customers. In addition, there are now a considerable number of these coarse papers transported to Jiaoji, Beining, and Longhai roads and lines. In order to fully develop road transportation, the three roads have been consulted and agreed to join this special rate for the joint transportation of coarse paper. The freight of each road part, except for the Longhai Road, which is still calculated according to the ordinary freight rate, the freight of the Jiaoji and Beining roads is calculated in accordance with the Jinpu and Jinghu-Huhangyong road methods, regardless of whether the vehicle is full or not, uniformly reduced by 10% according to the price listed in the current freight rate table, in order to absorb, etc." According to this, it is found that the special rate method for the joint transportation of coarse paper is said to be excellent during the trial period and should be approved to continue to extend the period for one year from January 1, 1936, in order to attract customers. In addition, the special rate has been agreed by the Zhejiang-Jiangxi Road to join Beining, Jiaoji, and Longhai Road, and it is approved to handle it accordingly. In addition to the separate order, it should be followed. This order has been transferred to the Transportation Department for compliance.

Due to the Wu Case, Discussing the Xuchang Tobacco Company, the Xuchang Court Ruled that the Lawsuit Would Not Be Prosecuted

According to Guowen News Agency, Mr. Wu Tingsheng, the former chairman of the Shanghai Chinese Cigarette Industry Association, was assassinated in Xuchang on the 30th of last month. All parties believe that there is a considerable relationship with the Xuchang Tobacco Company. A reporter met with the person in charge of the Cigarette Industry Association yesterday. According to the conversation, the outside world has been spreading that Mr. Wu's Xuchang Tobacco Company is an illegal organization, which is not true. Therefore, a copy of the non-prosecution decision issued by the Xuchang Local Court Inspection Office of Henan Province was produced to prove it. The original book is recorded as follows: Non-Prosecution Decision of the Xuchang Local Court Inspection Office of Henan Province. Defendant: Wu Tingsheng and other nine persons. Accuser: Jiang Zihe and other three persons. The right-listed defendants, etc., due to a case of financial fraud and embezzlement, was investigated and concluded by this office on No. 94 of the criminal investigation of the Republic of China, and it is considered that no prosecution should be initiated. The reasons in fact and law are as follows: Reasons in fact: Defendant Ren Boyan, in the early years of the Republic of China, purchased more than 90 mu of land from the Hu family and others outside the Xiguan of Xuchang in the name of Yongan Hall to build a factory to collect tobacco. He then leased it to the British-American Tobacco Company for a period of 30 years. The Ministry of Foreign Affairs believed that the contract was extremely harsh and violated Chinese sovereignty, and requested the Henan Provincial Government to instruct the Xuchang County Government to order Ren Boyan to amend the lease. Later, due to the outbreak of the war, the army was stationed for a long time and was not careful with fire, and all the houses were burned to the ground. The British-American Tobacco Company and Ren Boyan terminated the contract. However, the people of Xuchang still suspected that there were British and American foreign merchants as the background, and filed complaints with various central and local agencies for many years. After deliberation, the three departments of Foreign Affairs, Finance, and Industry convened a meeting, believing that since it had broken away from the British and Americans, the diplomatic issue could be declared over. In March of this summer, Ren Boyan again entrusted Shen Kunshan as an agent to sell the land to Xuchang Tobacco Leaf Co., Ltd., and there were new and old land deeds. Xuchang Company also registered No. 347 in the Ministry of Industry. The head office is located in Shanghai, and the Xuchang office has also been instructed by the Henan Provincial Government to supplement the branch registration. The company had long been legally established without foreign capital. Although there are preparations for the Yu-Su Baked Tobacco Factory recently, the nuclear volume has not been realized, and Jiang Zihe, etc., happened to file complaints twice at this time. Legal reasons: After verifying the repeated statements and county records of the accused Jiang Zihe, etc., it is considered that no prosecution should be initiated. The procedural and substantive laws are explained separately: Procedures are illegal. The regulations of the Criminal Procedure Law are clear from the accusation and report, and even ordinary people can understand. Since the accusers are not the victims themselves, how can they directly sue the court? Moreover, those who have already sued cannot report again, and it is also clearly stipulated in the same law. The accusers' statements that they stole and sold the national land, etc., have been reviewed, and there are no provisions in the criminal law. Assuming that it is one of the foreign troubles, it should be reported directly to the High Court, and this office can hardly accept it, and it can be directly rejected. However, the substantive law is not investigated, and it is not enough to convince and finalize the conviction. The substantive law is not unanimous. After reviewing the original copy, the accused Wu Tingsheng presented a volume of the new and old land deeds of the Xuchang Tobacco Leaf Company, Xiguan, outside Xuzhou City, Henan Province, in court on December 10 of this year. The procedures were complete and there were no flaws. The accusers are all making empty attacks, and the statements have no concrete evidence. It is difficult to think that there is a fact of buying and selling land on behalf of foreigners, and it is even more difficult to determine that the defendants are guilty. As for the middlemen Wang Yintang and Yang Ziming, they denied in court that they had signed, but after reviewing a letter sent by the defendant Xu Liwu from Kaifeng on November 28 of this year, it stated that in early February of this summer, Wu Tingsheng hosted a dinner at the company in Canghutong. Shen Kunshan, Chen Bo, Wang Yintang, Zhu Youlian, Zhou Jintang, Yang Ziming, and the speaker, as well as two people in the company, were at the same table. Wu Tingsheng said at the table that the land had been sold to Xuchang Company by Shen Kunshan on behalf of the company. All the gentlemen are here to witness, etc., which proves that the defendants Wang Yintang and Yang Ziming were also present and cannot deny it. After comparing the handwriting of Yang Ziming's letter to Wu Tingsheng and Wu Shenpeng with the six characters of Wang Yintang and Yang Ziming signed on the original contract, there is no difference, and the testimony of the defendant Yang Ziming is obviously flawed and difficult to believe. Furthermore, the witnesses are one of the essential elements of a private contract, and they are also to witness the dispute between the two parties. If both parties acknowledge it, it does not have any relationship with the third party, and it is unreasonable for the accusers to use this as an attack target. Based on the above conclusion, the conduct of the accused Wu Tingsheng, etc., does not constitute a crime, and no prosecution should be initiated in accordance with Article 231, Section 8 of the Criminal Law. A special disposition is made as follows: Prosecutor Jing Huimin, Clerk Li Xiaozeng.

Shareholders of Yichang and Yikang Money Shops, etc., Yan Ruling Petitions for Reconciliation, The Court Specially Convened a Meeting of Creditors to Decide on the Creditor Program

After the collapse of Yichang and Yikang Money Shops and Yifengchang Silk Shop in this city last year, Yan Ruling, the shareholder of the shops, filed a petition with the Shanghai First Special District Local Court to apply for reconciliation. The court accepted the case and appointed accountant Li Ding and lawyer Zhang Shirang as supervisors and assistants. At 3 pm the day before yesterday, a meeting of creditors was convened at the office of accountant Li at No. 133 Yuanmingyuan Road. The situation is recorded as follows:

Creditors Attending: Yu Lüde, a judge of the First Special Court, attended; supervisors and assistants Li Ding and Zhang Shirang attended; debtor Yan Ruling attended; and creditors Wu Zitai of the Youth Company, representing a debt of 28,000 yuan, Yan Xiyu of the Continental Bank, representing a debt of 20,000 yuan, and Zhou Bingrong, the liquidator of Yifengchang, representing a debt of 462,637.45 yuan, and Xu Boxiong, representing the creditor of Yichang Zhuang, representing a debt of 600,716.8 yuan.

Meeting Situation: Judge Yu, Li Ding, and Zhang Shirang served as the presidium. Judge Yu first reported the purpose of convening the creditors' meeting, followed by accountant Li Ding reporting the number of debt declarations and registrations, and the number of creditors attending today and the amount of debt represented. Finally, the declaration of the reconciliation plan applied for by debtor Yan Ruling was read out. The creditors attending believed that there was still a need to study the reconciliation plan, so Judge Yu announced that the creditors should first study the plan, and then the court would convene a meeting of creditors to vote for or against the decision.

Reconciliation Plan: The reconciliation plan proposed by debtor Yan Ruling is recorded as follows: Inquiry: The estimated cash assets of Yan Ruling are about 962,695.8 yuan, and the estimated recoverable amount is only 346,695.8 yuan. When the actual price is realized, there will be differences between the estimated recoverable amount and the estimated amount. As for the current liabilities, the total is 1,700,719.95 yuan, of which 596,000 yuan of secured priority debts can be disposed of the collateral to obtain compensation, and the unsecured ordinary debts are 1,091,194.93 yuan. The estimated recoverable amount of 346,695.8 yuan is not enough to offset the shortfall of 744,499.13 yuan. The shortfall is so large that Yan Ruling has no other assets to clear the debt, and he has no choice but to distribute the estimated recoverable amount of 346,695.8 yuan of assets on average to the unsecured ordinary debts of 1,091,194.93 yuan, and each debt of 100 yuan can be assigned 31.77 yuan. If the recoverable amount of the estimated price is more, the number of percentages distributed on average can be slightly increased. If the price is less, the number of percentages assigned can only be slightly reduced. There is no alternative, and there is no good plan. Therefore, the method of averaging the price of assets is used as a reconciliation plan. I beg your court to review and approve it and send it to the creditors for the creditors' meeting to decide whether to approve it or not. Petitioner: Yan Ruling, Accountant: Xu Yongzuo.

Dance Halls Levy Aviation Donation: All Dance Halls Implemented Yesterday; Collection Method of One Jiao and Five Fen Approved by Municipal Government and Concession Authorities

The China Aviation Association petitioned the municipal government for approval and received support from the Public Concession and French Concession authorities. It was decided to start collecting the Aviation Patriotic Donation from dance halls beginning on the 5th of this month. For dance halls selling dance tickets with fewer than six tickets per yuan, a tax of one jiao will be collected per customer; for six or more tickets per yuan, a tax of five fen will be collected. The tax will be collected when the bill is presented. All dance halls have already implemented this measure. Details are as follows:

Notice of Implementation: Our association is organizing the collection of Aviation Patriotic Funds in all city dance halls. We previously petitioned the Shanghai Municipal Government for support and received strong assistance from the two Concession authorities. Since the trial implementation began on August 15th of last year, the results have been excellent. To facilitate the process, we have specially revised the method to be collected by the dance halls when presenting the bill. For dance halls selling dance tickets with fewer than six tickets per yuan, a tax of one jiao (big coin) will be collected per customer; for six or more tickets per yuan, a tax of five fen (big coin) will be collected. This will officially begin on January 5th. We hope that compatriots from all walks of life will contribute generously, comply with the regulations, and gather strength to achieve the goal of Aviation Patriotic efforts. The future of the nation and people truly relies on this. This notice is hereby issued.

Collection Method: The China Aviation Association has established this method to widely raise Aviation Patriotic Funds: All dance businesses, whether halls or schools using dance tickets, are subject to collection. For dance halls selling dance tickets with fewer than six tickets per yuan, a tax of one jiao (big coin) will be collected per customer; for six or more tickets per yuan, a tax of five fen will be collected. Dance hall businesses will collect the Aviation Donation when presenting the bill. The collection of Aviation Patriotic Funds by dance hall businesses is limited to 100,000 yuan. The China Aviation Association will print a two-part receipt book for dance businesses collecting Aviation Patriotic Donations. The first part will be given to the customer when paying the bill. The China Aviation Association may send personnel to inspect the collection situation at various dance halls at any time. Each dance hall should settle the collected donations every five days and send them to the office of the Shanghai City Solicitation Team Headquarters of the China Aviation Association for verification. The China Aviation Association should publicly announce the amount of donations received from each dance hall at the end of each month. This method has been submitted to the government for approval and implementation.

Lu Yuelian from Huzhou and Luo Xinfang from Yong, residents of No. 113 Datong Road, secretly peddled various aviation lottery tickets with altered expiry dates of the 18th issue at reduced prices at the Wanxing Teahouse, No. 827 North Chengdu Road, on the morning of the 3rd of this month. Flesh and Blood: Laborer's Right Hand Crushed; Bone Fractures May Cause Disability

Shen Luoxi, a 26-year-old laborer from Jiangbei, worked at the Hexing Copper Smelting Factory located at the intersection of Ningwu Road and Hejian Road. Shooting Battle During Robbery Arrest at the Intersection of Rue Baille: One Robber Wounded and Captured

At around 0:45 AM this morning, a pedestrian was passing behind the cow slaughtering company at the South Zhujiaqiao in the French Concession when four thugs suddenly emerged from the darkness, brandishing pistols, and blocked his path. The robbers opened fire to resist arrest, and the patrol officer also drew his gun and returned fire. More than ten shots were fired, like a string of pearls. As a result, one of the robbers in blue cloth shirt and pants was shot in the lower body and collapsed. He was arrested by the patrol officer and taken to the Songshan Road Police Station together with the victim for further investigation. The remaining robbers managed to escape without a trace.

Railway Bureau: Regulations for Calculating Through Ticket Fares

The Lianglu Railway Administration stated that since the Jinpu Railway reduced passenger ticket prices from January 1st of this year, the previously issued through ticket fare tables from other connecting railway bureaus are no longer applicable. The Transportation Department is currently re-compiling them. Before the revised through ticket fare tables are printed and issued, each connecting station will temporarily compile its own through ticket fare tables for use. To avoid calculation errors, the following calculation methods have been established:

Ordinary Trains: (1) Ordinary trains, via the old ferry. (A) One-way ticket, for example, Shanghai to Beiping. The ordinary ticket price from Shanghai to Nanjing should be added to the ordinary ticket price from the capital to Tianjin, and then the ordinary ticket price from Tianjin to Beiping. For example, if it is first class, it is 9 yuan, 4 jiao, 5 fen, plus 45 yuan, 6 jiao, plus 6 yuan, 3 jiao, totaling 61 yuan, 3 jiao, 5 fen. (B) Round-trip sightseeing ticket, for example, Shanghai to Beiping round-trip. The ordinary round-trip ticket price between Shanghai and Nanjing should be added to the ordinary round-trip ticket price between the capital and Tianjin, and then the ordinary round-trip ticket price between Tianjin and Beiping. For example, if it is first class, it is 14 yuan, 2 jiao between Shanghai and Nanjing, plus 68 yuan, 4 jiao between the capital and Tianjin, plus 9 yuan, 4 jiao, 5 fen between Tianjin and Beiping, totaling 92 yuan, 0 jiao, 5 fen.

Special Express Trains: (2) Special express trains, via railway ferry. (A) One-way ticket, for example, Shanghai to Beiping first class. The ticket price should be calculated according to item (1) A, which is 61 yuan, 3 jiao, 5 fen, plus the difference between the old and new ferries of 4 jiao, 5 fen, plus the first-class special express train surcharge of 9 yuan for the through mileage of 1462 kilometers between Shanghai and Beiping, totaling 70 yuan, 8 jiao. (B) Round-trip sightseeing ticket, for example, Shanghai to Beiping round-trip first class. The round-trip ticket price from Shanghai to Nanjing of 14 yuan, 2 jiao should be added to the round-trip ticket price from Nanjing to Tianjin of 14 yuan, 2 jiao, the round-trip ticket price from Nanjing to Tianjin of 68 yuan, 2 jiao, the round-trip ticket price from Tianjin to Beiping of 9 yuan, 4 jiao, 5 fen, plus the special express train surcharge for the round-trip through mileage of 18 yuan, and the round-trip ferry fee of 1 yuan, 2 jiao, totaling 111 yuan, 0 jiao, 5 fen.

Gu Xiangzhou Commits Suicide by Poison

Gu Xiangzhou, also known as Shengzu, a 30-year-old man from Zhoupu Town, Nanhui, was from a well-to-do family. His parents were healthy. He married the daughter of the owner of Jiahelong Rice Store outside Xiaonanmen in this city. Gu used to work in the exchange but had recently been unemployed. For some unknown reason, he suddenly had a moment of short-sightedness. On the evening of December 30th of last year, he went to the Renhe Inn at No. 114 Dongzilaihuo Street in the French Concession and rented Room 28. That night, he committed suicide by poisoning himself. He had notified his family in advance. The next day at noon, the porter, Li Dangtian, knocked on the door to urge him to get up and discovered that he had been poisoned and was unconscious. He immediately reported it to the police station. Wei sent him to Guangci Hospital for treatment, but it was ineffective, and he died that day. The police station sent the body to the autopsy site. Because it was the New Year, the court was on vacation. When his elderly father, Gu Liankui, received the news and rushed to Shanghai to visit, Gu had already died. On the morning of the 4th, the police station reported it to Wang Ren, the prosecutor of the Second Special Court, who, along with the medical officer and clerk, went to the site to confirm the cause of death. The father claimed the body and coffin and transported them back to his hometown for burial.

1936 China Insurance Yearbook Begins Pre-Order

The China Insurance Yearbook Society, recognizing the backwardness of the insurance industry in China and believing that the crux of the problem lies in the lack of insurance statistics, has collaborated with the China Life Insurance Advancement Society to hire experts to compile an insurance yearbook to provide reference for those engaged in insurance and those studying insurance in China. The 1935 Insurance Yearbook was published in April of last year. Due to its abundant materials and accurate statistics, it has been widely praised by readers. People in the insurance industry, finance industry, libraries, business students, and those interested in the insurance industry have all eagerly purchased it. Sales have reached thousands of copies, which can be said to be a positive development in the midst of the economic downturn. Now, the 1936 China Insurance Yearbook is being compiled again. The content is divided into two parts: the main compilation and the appendix. The main compilation has ten chapters, including: The recent year's development of the insurance industry in China; A general overview of insurance companies nationwide; Surveys of the insurance industry in various regions; Insurance organizations; Insurance laws and regulations; Insurance statistics; Definitions of insurance terms; A directory of people in insurance companies; Insurance diaries; An index of insurance treatises. The appendix has four chapters, including: A general overview of the insurance industry in various countries; Business surveys of foreign companies in China; Developments of foreign companies in the past year; Foreign insurance associations. It is said that the compilation is being conducted very carefully, and the selection of materials is particularly precise, so the content is rich and can meet the needs of the general public. It can be predicted that the society has separated and become independent from the China Life Insurance Advancement Society, which contains foreign company components, to avoid misunderstandings from the outside world. The society's address is No. 7 Tongchun Lane, Baker Road, and its official name is China Insurance Yearbook Society. However, the society is now carrying out this arduous task with the efforts of a few people, and their enthusiasm is commendable. Therefore, all sectors are providing assistance to reward them for their hard work in serving the Chinese insurance industry. The pre-order started on the 1st and was originally scheduled to end on the 15th. The price is four yuan, and the pre-order price is two yuan. To avoid disappointment for distant readers, it has been decided to extend the deadline by half a month. Therefore, it is expected that it will cause a sensation at that time, with people rushing to pre-order.

Strange Incident Amidst Anti-Smoking Campaign: Photograph Published Claiming Addiction Recovery; Hospital Advertisement Uses Any Means to Promote It; Non-Smoker Falsely Accused of Recovering from Addiction – Chen Huihong Sues Sun Jianmin for Defamation –

Sun Jianmin, a man from Shaoxing in his thirties, established Renhe Hospital at No. 191 Avenue Petain at the intersection of Avenue Joffre in the French Concession (opposite the Franco-Chinese School), serving as its director. He has recently been sued for defamation by Chen Huihong, a fellow doctor (29 years old, from Guangdong, and the chief physician at Ren Ci Hospital at the intersection of Avenue Edward VII and Rue du Consulat), who, along with lawyers Jiang Yiping and Wu Baotai, filed a complaint with the Criminal Division of the Special District Court, seeking investigation and requesting compensation of two thousand yuan. The complaint alleges that the Renhe Hospital, established by the defendant, published an advertisement promoting smoking cessation on a certain newspaper on December 4th, which included several half-body photographs of people who had supposedly quit opium. The defendant placed the plaintiff's photograph as the eighth person in the bottom row, with the caption "Photo for Testimony, Real Name Omitted." The content further stated that "the above gentlemen all quit in October and received certificates from the rehabilitation center. Their photos will be published monthly for identification by fellow smokers." The plaintiff was astonished and outraged. He leads a clean and self-respecting life without any addictions. The defendant, formerly known as Sun Huilin, worked as a staff member in the Daxue Pharmacy established by the plaintiff's father and knows him well. The defendant is fully aware of the plaintiff's family background and appearance. Now, the defendant unscrupulously sacrifices the reputation of others as a tool to expand his publicity and achieve the goal of deceiving the public. The plaintiff feels deeply pained and has been reprimanded by his elders and advised by friends, as if the accusation were true, causing the plaintiff immense shame and significant damage to his reputation and mental well-being. The Special District Court Judge Sun Peng conducted a hearing, during which the defendant, Sun Jianmin, argued that the photograph was mistakenly sent to the newspaper for publication by the clerk, Shen Zixiang, due to temporary oversight, and that he has filed a separate lawsuit against Shen Zixiang for negligence. He also hired a lawyer for his defense. The court ordered the defendant to post bail and entrusted his lawyer to secure his release, pending a rescheduled hearing. The Special District Court has already concluded the trial of Sun Jianmin's suit against the clerk Shen Zixiang, acquitting Shen Zixiang. The court has scheduled a continued hearing for today morning in Chen Huihong's lawsuit against Sun Jianmin for defamation. It is rumored that relatives and friends of both parties have intervened, and Sun Jianmin has published an apology to the plaintiff in the newspaper, leading to a settlement and the plaintiff's withdrawal of the lawsuit.

Seventh District Branch of the Municipal Federation of Trade Unions Holds Fifth Membership Meeting Yesterday; Liu Zhongying and Others Elected to Executive Committee

The Seventh District Branch of the Municipal Federation of Trade Unions in the First Special District of this city held its fifth membership meeting at its office yesterday to elect new executive committee members. Over seventy people attended, including Zhu Yangwu, a representative from the Municipal Party Headquarters, Zhang Qingyun, a representative from the Municipal General Chamber of Commerce, Zhang Xianfang, Zhu Baoluo, Chen Jiufeng, Ge Futian, Zhu Yutao, and Xu Zhaode from various district branches, as well as other members. Liu Zhongying, Zhou Fuwei, and Xu Tingzu were publicly elected as the presidium. They reported on the purpose of the meeting and the work situation of the association. Following this, Zhu Yangwu, a representative from the Municipal Party Headquarters, and Zhang Qingyun, a representative from the Municipal General Chamber of Commerce, gave encouraging speeches and guidance. The election results were as follows: Liu Zhongying, Shi Jiulin, Xu Tingzu, Wu Hongsheng, Xiang Liansun, Tong Decheng, Jian Yujie, Zhou Fuwei, Chen Xiaoqin, Liu Chunhua, Lu Deming, Chen Yuanxing, Cai Liqing, Chen Baowen, and Zhang Fangbiao were elected as executive committee members. Liu Gengxin, Fei Fuqing, Zhou Jisheng, Pan Youfeng, and Hou Xiangliu were elected as alternate executive committee members. They took their oaths of office on the spot. The meeting discussed the following proposals: - Telegraphed the government to promptly order the suppression of rebels and the preservation of territory. - Petitioned the Executive Yuan and the Ministry of Foreign Affairs of the National Government to negotiate with Japan to stop the issuance of banknotes in Shanghai. - Actively promoted domestic goods. - Petitioned the Municipal Government to promptly issue rent reductions to alleviate the people's difficulties. - Members jointly reported that the owner, Yeguang Company, disregarded the suffering of tenants and arbitrarily sued for rent arrears. The meeting adjourned with refreshments.

City Voices

Tap Dance Expert Dick Opens Classes: Tap dance was invented by Black people, it is a kind of dance, beautiful and exciting. It is often seen in musical films. Many Chinese people enjoy this style but do not know where to learn it, which is a great regret. They often go through many people asking for introductions and paying a dozen yuan an hour to study. In the end, they achieve nothing, wasting time and money. This is because the teacher is used to performing for a living, and once they switch to teaching, they do not know the proper method, and the students give up because it is too difficult. Now, dance instructor Mr. Dick has studied this dance for many years and has mastered its secrets. He has rich teaching experience and his teaching method is detailed and clear, making it easy for people to understand. Anyone with a little musical knowledge can learn it. The tuition is low, and there are two types of classes: general classes and individual classes. Enrollment has already begun. The school address is No. 420 Avenue Foch, diagonally opposite the Jiuxing Cinema.

Guanghua Optical Company Holds New Year Guessing Game: Guanghua Optical Company, an expert in eyeglasses in this city, is holding a guessing game to increase the New Year's interest of people from all walks of life. The method is simple, anyone can participate, and everyone has the hope of winning cash and valuable eyeglass lenses. In this game, Guanghua Optical Company will pre-place eight kinds of famous lenses, such as (Crookes), (Kroksheet), (Roosevelt), into eight paper bags numbered from one to eight, and give them to lawyer Liu Weilun for safekeeping. Participants only need to guess what kind of lens is in which numbered bag. If it matches the original completely, they can get 20 yuan in national currency. The closest guesses or those who do not guess correctly also have the hope of getting Huermu, Zeiss, or Crookes lenses, or other gifts. Entry tickets can be obtained free of charge from the Guanghua headquarters, the south branch, the west branch, and the north branch, or a blank piece of paper filled in will also be valid. Since the company started its big discount and cash giveaway, it has been truly genuine and offered thorough sacrifices, so customers are crowding and the store is bustling. It is said that the discount period will soon expire, so all circles should not miss this good opportunity.

"Hursol" Asthma Medicine Sells Well: German "Felsol" Hursol asthma medicine, specializing in treating asthma, shortness of breath, difficulty breathing, asthma caused by chronic bronchitis or heart disease, acute heart pain, various heart diseases, chronic coughs, whooping cough, influenza and other symptoms, is manufactured by the "Lohmann" Pharmaceutical Factory in Essen, Germany. Throughout China, the sole general agent is the Huashang Luying Western Medicine Company at No. 150 Jiujiang Road, Shanghai. Now that it is the height of winter and the weather is severe, orders from major pharmacies in the city and other places are overwhelming. It is said that "Hursol" is packaged in three types: large boxes selling for 3 yuan in national currency, small boxes selling for 1.60 yuan in national currency, and trial packs selling for 0.80 yuan. You can order directly from the pharmacy, and large boxes, small boxes, and trial packs are all sold in major pharmacies in this city.

Calligraphy and Painting News

Annual Offering of Calligraphy Couplets and Paintings for the Entire Hall: Zhang Dan'an, a calligrapher from Lanling, due to the approaching Lunar New Year, when various circles are preparing items for decorating their reception rooms, is exceptionally offering a thousand paintings. For each couplet or central hanging scroll within five feet, he charges a nominal fee of one yuan for the ink. For a four-panel screen, he charges two yuan. To better serve customers, he is offering an additional couplet with his signature. Those who order a central hanging scroll, a couplet, and a set of screens will be considered as ordering a complete set ("entire hall") and, in addition to the free couplet, will receive an additional 20% discount on the already low prices. This offer is valid until the end of the lunar year and will not be extended. Postage stamps are accepted, and paper is provided. Payments can be forwarded through the Yaxdong Bank on Tianjin Road, Shanghai.

After the publication of the first volume, it was highly praised by scholars at home and abroad. The entire book is set in Nos. 4 and 5 type, line-inserted, and the layout is sparse and elegant. The price is extremely low, with each volume costing 50 cents for the popular edition and 70 cents for the special edition. The entire set is only four yuan, which is much cheaper than the twenty or thirty yuan required for just one volume of "Yuan Qu Xuan." It is said that the series has now published eighteen titles and is published every Saturday without delay. Next week's book will be Li Liweng's "Xian Qing Ou Ji," which is very interesting, with humorous writing and bizarre ideas, accompanied by more than a dozen illustrations.

Weather Report

The Xujiahui Observatory's meteorological report at 4:30 PM yesterday stated that the weather around Shandong is clear and cold, with northwest to north winds of varying degrees. The Yangtze River basin and this area are cloudy and cold, with local snow, gradually becoming cloudy, with morning fog and northwest to northeast breezes of varying degrees. The East China Sea is cloudy, with rain and gentle cyclones, due to a low-pressure system moving northeastward. Also, in the 24 hours before 3:00 PM yesterday, the highest temperature in this city was 42.1 degrees and the lowest was 32.2 degrees. On the same day last year, the highest temperature was 41.5 degrees and the lowest was 23.9 degrees.

A Visit to the Jiufu Pharmaceutical Company

— Qian Hua

The Jiufu Pharmaceutical Company on Baker Road in this city has launched a new drug, a spleen-lung hormone preparation called "Pisu," opening a new era in Western medicine. Our reporter made a special visit and was personally greeted by Manager Zhu Duanfu. After a brief exchange of pleasantries, he led the reporter to the manufacturing plant's office. Although the office was small, the arrangement was quite neat and clean. Through Mr. Zhu's introduction, the reporter also met the factory director, Mr. Hu Zhenhan, and the deputy factory director, Mr. Wang Shirong. Together, they took the reporter to tour the factory. The factory is divided into two parts: one is for manufacturing various finished products, located on the lower lip, and the other is for specialized manufacturing of injectable medicines, located on the second floor. The reporter first went to the finished product manufacturing area and saw various machines in operation. The sound of the machines was deafening. Under the guidance of Factory Directors Hu and Wang, the reporter learned the purpose of each machine, such as the Sharples ultra-high-speed centrifuge used to manufacture "Bulido," the mixer for extracting "Jiufu Gadger," and the vacuum distillation machine. According to Mr. Hu, the raw material for extracting "Gadger" is cod liver oil, from which about 1.5 to 2.0% of "Gadger" can be extracted, which is then used to mix with "Bulido" to enhance its nourishing function. Therefore, the effectiveness of "Bulido" can be imagined. In addition, there are also alkalizing machines, vacuum extraction machines, steam boilers, stone mills, and cod liver oil mixing machines, all used for manufacturing various finished products. A ultraviolet light room is also set aside in the corner of the field to manufacture Vitamin D. It is said that this is the initial work of manufacturing "Purple Light Malt Cod Liver Oil." Going further inside, the reporter saw an even larger area with more machines, including machines for manufacturing "Bailing Ji," "Milky White Cod Liver Oil," and "Sheng Dan," including a grinder, a powder mixer, a granule mixer, a sand grain manufacturing machine, a powder separator, a tray-type vacuum dryer, a tablet sorter, and eighteen tablet-making machines, occupying one-third of the entire area. There are also powder combination machines for making pills, pill-kneading machines, pill-making machines, coating machines, polishing machines, milky white cod liver oil mixing machines, oil-refining machines, and the latest type of Colin's oil combination machines. Outside the factory is the boiler room where the steam boilers are located. Then, the reporter exited the factory, climbed the stairs, and visited the injection manufacturing department. Upon reaching the second floor, the words "Clinic" were displayed horizontally in front of the reporter. The reporter inquired about the clinic's recent situation, and Manager Zhu invited the reporter into the room and showed X-ray images and temperature charts of patients with various stages of lung disease cured by "Pisu," and informed the reporter of "Pisu's" antipyretic effect on tuberculosis, as well as its cough-suppressing and weight-gain effects. At this time, poor and sick patients waiting for consultation outside the room were already standing by. The reporter then went straight to visit the rooms for manufacturing "Pisu." The rooms were all adjacent to the road, with sufficient light. From the storage of animal spleens to the manufacture of Pisu, a total of nine rooms are used. A rectangular porcelain sign is hung on the door, with the name of the department on it. The first is the raw material cold storage room, which is dedicated to storing animal spleens, using scientific refrigeration equipment to prevent spleen corruption. The second is the autopsy and organ component separation room. The initial work of "Pisu" is to dissect the spleen, extract and separate the active ingredients, and then go to the third room to dry them. After drying, the crude products are first manufactured in the fourth room, and then the crude products are placed in the centrifuge in the fifth room so that all the impurities in the spleen are separated by centrifugal force, and then sent to the sixth room for refining. After refining, the finished "Pisu" is then sent to the seventh room to be placed in ampoules, and then to the eighth room for disinfection. Once the disinfection is completed, the manufacturing process is completed. However, in order to determine the titer, a ninth room is specially set up for determining the titer and research. After inspection, it can be packaged and sold. The reporter was limited by time and did not have time to visit the packaging animal two rooms, so he bid farewell and returned. The factory has sophisticated machinery and a meticulous organization. What can be seen in the above can be seen. It is said that all the major doctors in Shanghai will be invited to visit to seek help from other mountains.

Beiping Universities to Start Winter Vacation Early; Peking University Plans to Resume Classes Today

(Central News Agency, Beiping, 5th) The universities in Beiping were originally scheduled to resume classes on the 4th, but due to the firm attitude of the students, this did not happen. It is now reported that Tsinghua, Yenching, Dongda, Teachers College, and other schools will begin their winter vacation early from the 6th. Peking University plans to resume classes on the 6th. The authorities of Pingda University are further persuading the students. In addition, the United Association of Private Middle Schools in Beiping has nominated Wu Jian and others as representatives to go to Nanjing to meet with President Chiang Kai-shek to listen to his instructions. The list has been submitted to the Bureau of Social Affairs for review.

(Beiping, 5th) The universities in Beiping have been boycotting classes for a long time. In addition to Tsinghua, which began its vacation yesterday, Teachers College, Jiaotong University, Northeastern University, and others have also successively issued vacation announcements. Peking University and Pingda University are continuing to persuade students because the majority of students support resuming classes. The private universities have not yet decided on a method for the issue of vacation or resumption of classes. The authorities of the schools in the city are scheduled to go to Nanjing together around the 10th to visit Chiang Kai-shek.

Chen Lijang Discusses Impressions of Inspecting Education in the Southwest (Part 1)

Mr. Chen Lijang was previously hired by the Ministry of Education to inspect education in the southwestern provinces. He departed from the capital for Sichuan in October of last year, inspected Sichuan for a month, then flew from Chongqing to Guizhou. After completing his duties in Guizhou, he continued by plane to Yunnan for inspection, spending a total of three months. It is learned that Mr. Chen returned to the capital yesterday. Since the founding of the Republic, the Ministry of Education has not sent personnel to inspect the education of Sichuan, Guizhou, and Yunnan, except for Sichuan. This time, Mr. Chen braved the long journey to conduct a detailed inspection. Now that he has returned safely, it is believed that Mr. Chen will have concrete suggestions for the future improvement of education in the Southwest to contribute to the central government. Therefore, our reporter paid a special visit to Mr. Chen at his residence. He appeared energetic despite his recent travels. After shaking hands and exchanging pleasantries, the reporter immediately inquired about the situation of education in Sichuan, Guizhou, and Yunnan. Mr. Chen's statements are as follows: "I was ordered by the Ministry of Education to inspect education in Sichuan, Guizhou, and Yunnan for three months. I will submit a separate report to the Ministry regarding the detailed current situation of education at all levels in the three provinces and the points that should be improved. Now, I will briefly describe the education situation in the three provinces as follows:

(1) Sichuan: Sichuan's politics have been extremely dark in the past twenty years. Since the reorganization of the provincial government last year, everything in Sichuan has gradually been on track under the guidance of the central government. However, due to years of war and social economy, it is completely bankrupt. Therefore, the educational funding at all levels is very stretched, and the equipment is extremely simple. The specific details are as follows: (A) Sichuan University: It is undeniable that the past management was not good. Since Ren Hongjun was ordered to be the president, he has been determined to improve it, such as the employment of full-time professors, the enrichment of courses, and the purchase of books. Now, in order to make the school the highest institution of higher learning in the Southwest and cultivate talents, the central government has allocated 2.6 million yuan for the construction of school buildings and various scientific research equipment. Therefore, the future of Sichuan University is very optimistic. Secondly, the private West China University is well-managed, especially its dentistry department, which is the most famous. The museum attached to the school has a rich collection. As for Chongqing University, it has gradually improved since Hu Shuhua took over. (B) Sichuan Middle Schools: There are currently more than 270 schools. Although the number is large, the funding is uncertain and the equipment is very simple. Moreover, some counties have diverted funds from primary education to run middle schools. Therefore, in several counties, there are more middle schools than complete primary schools. This kind of畸形development has been discussed with the Education Department to formulate standards and find ways to improve it. (C) Sichuan primary school education is very bad due to poor local security and lack of funding in the past. If you want to make progress, you must try to rectify it. As for the short-term primary schools that have been reported for establishment, there are only more than 90 counties, and more than 50 counties are still missing. This is because although the central government issued a subsidy of 140,000 yuan this time, the provincial treasury did not raise a single point, and the local government only used the remaining administrative fees from the abolished bureaus to abolish the short-term primary schools, and this number is also very small and uncertain. I have consulted with the provincial authorities and asked them to find ways to raise funds and urge the counties to quickly establish short-term primary schools to comply with the central government's decree.

(2) Guizhou: Guizhou is poor and its people are poor. In addition, the past rulers were extremely plundering. The social economy is in an unthinkable state of depression. Since the reorganization of the provincial government last year, all undertakings have begun to have clues. Now the Education Department has plans for the province's educational facilities. The situation of education at all levels can be described as follows: (A) There is no higher education to speak of in Guizhou. As for secondary education, the school equipment is extremely poor. Each secondary school (rarely has student dormitories, and other things can be imagined). In addition, there is a lack of talent. Some teachers teach concurrently in several schools, and the number of teaching hours per week is as high as more than 36 hours. Currently, provincial middle schools are only in the provincial capital, and the funding is provided by the Education Department. As for the provincial middle schools in other counties, although they are called provincial schools, the funding is jointly raised by several counties. Now, after consultation with the Education Department, it is decided that student dormitories in each middle school must be built in stages, and the equipment must be enriched. Teachers who teach concurrently must be strictly investigated. The funding for provincial middle schools in each county should be borne by the provincial treasury, and the remaining funds should be returned to each county to run primary education. (B) Primary schools in Guizhou are even less developed, and the teachers' salaries are very low. As for the short-term primary schools, the central government subsidized 160,000 yuan, and the provincial government also raised 147,000 yuan (including Miao education funds). The province used this fund to run 615 short-term primary schools. Each school stipulates 250 yuan and runs a compulsory education experimental area. Because the education treatment of short-term primary schools is higher than that of ordinary primary schools, and there is money, the short-term primary schools are well-managed. (C) The Han and Miao people live together in Guizhou. The number of Miao people accounts for more than one-third of the province's population. Since Chairman Chiang advocated Miao education in Guizhou, the Education Department has also formulated a plan. In addition to short-term primary schools that also accept Miao children, six provincial primary schools have been established in the areas where the most Miao people live in the province, such as Libo, Danjiang, and Shuicheng, to specifically recruit Miao people. Another rural normal school has been established to train teachers for Miao education. A junior high school is attached to the school as a place for Miao children who are interested in further education. All are being actively carried out. The purpose of this education is to break down the barriers between the Han and Miao people and enable them to receive education with the Han people, so that they can be subtly influenced and effective invisibly. However, the living conditions, habits, and languages of Miao students are very different from those of Han people. Therefore, how to consider the gains and losses of the curriculum and teaching materials still needs our research.

Anhui Province Implements Mobile Teaching Method

In order to promote compulsory education by using mobile teaching, Anhui Province has designated 10,000 yuan from the compulsory education fund for the 24th year to implement mobile teaching. Mobile teaching is carried out on a trial basis in villages with vast areas and inconvenient transportation. The required teachers are selected from normal students or registered and qualified primary school teachers. The mobile teachers are paid 150 yuan per year, and travel expenses are paid separately. When departing, they carry a mobile library for work. Each teacher is required to teach in three villages in rotation, and stay in each village for at least one week, teaching ten students. The Baojia chiefs are responsible for raising classrooms and teacher accommodation locally. The county governments issue orders to their subordinates to protect the mobile teachers and assist them in their teaching work. The mobile teachers are assessed and supervised by the county education authorities and submit a monthly report on their teaching to the relevant authorities for filing.

Children's Educational Novel

Little Men (1) (4) (3)

— Original by Louisa M. Alcott Translated by Zheng Xiaocang

Moore repeated the story of his loss. Mr. Bae listened, his face gradually becoming serious, because although the children had many minor faults before, they had not been fake.

"You sit down," he said, after everyone was seated, his gaze shifted from one face to another, a look of misery that was more uncomfortable to see than a scolding, while slowly saying:

"Children, now I want to ask each person a simple question, I only ask for an honest answer, I do not want to use intimidation, tricks, or cunning means to find out the truth of this matter; each of you has a conscience. The person who offended Tao Moore now has his chance to seek remedy and to repent before us all. I think it is sometimes excusable to be tempted by temporary desire, but cheating is different. So do not add lying to stealing, or confess clearly so we can try to help you make us forget about it."

He paused for a moment, and the room was silent; then he slowly and solemnly asked this question of each person, although each person's please was a little different, the whole made the same answer. Each face was flushed, showing excitement, so Mr. Bae could not take the color as a sign. Several children were so flustered that they could not utter the simple words, as if they were guilty of a crime, but it was clear that they would not. When he asked Ned, he especially softened his voice, because the poor child looked so bitter, and Mr. Bae felt sympathy for him. He believed that he was a criminal, and hoped that the child would not dare to lie again, so he used an attitude of friendship to enable him to fearlessly tell the truth.

A List of Chinese Public Bonds in the 25th Year of the Republic of China

This publication lists and discloses the repayment of principal and interest of various central and local, domestic and foreign bonds over the past year, as well as their current status, which readers find quite convenient.
