Securities: The Bond Market at the Year-End and Beginning

Initially Sold Off Heavily by Financial Institutions, but Ultimately Recovered Due to Short Covering by Retail Investors

Last week was the end of the 24th year of the Republic and the beginning of the 25th year, and the transition showed a different trend of volatility. At the year-end and beginning, there was a proposal for Japanese merchants to use Japanese currency in China, which was subsequently halted due to disagreement from the Japanese consulate, and market prices were once again shaken. This led to a strong rebound in the market. The situation in North China is becoming increasingly complex, and the overall adjustment is said to be underway. The public bond market has experienced many storms, and market sentiment is accustomed to it. If an event is not of significant severity, market prices are not affected by it, which shows the stability of market sentiment. The larger fluctuations in market prices occur during the anticipation of an event, and once it becomes clear, market prices stabilize. Take the currency reform as an example, the trends before and after the event were completely different. It is not that the event has changed, but rather that the balance of power in terms of capital has shifted to one side, and any excess or deficiency is enough to shake the market. Currently, the market is characterized by long positions held by retail investors and short positions held by large institutions. The environment is unlikely to undergo any major changes that would significantly affect the market, but infighting is inevitable due to the large volume of transactions and the short time frame. Last week only had three trading days. On Monday, financial institutions and gold merchants sold off, and the selling pressure from a large institution surnamed Sheng was also strong. This was compounded by the proposal for Japanese merchants to use Japanese currency, which was enough to shake the unification of China's currency. Market prices fell by several jiao to about one yuan, and then immediately rebounded. As a result, prices recovered by 1-2 jiao to 6-7 jiao. Wednesday to Friday were New Year's holidays and trading was suspended. On Saturday, the market opened strong and sentiment was excellent. The No. 43 representative bought on behalf of various groups, and retail investors also rushed to cover their short positions, resulting in a very positive trend and strong upward momentum, with prices soaring by several jiao to over two yuan. However, it was felt that the upward momentum was too sharp and difficult to sustain. As a result, prices rose by 2-3 jiao to 2.3 yuan. The total transaction volume was 63.53 million yuan. The results of the price increases and decreases are listed in the table on the left (unit: yuan, transaction unit: hundred yuan).

Yarn and Cotton: Overseas Cotton Market Reverses and Falls

Yesterday, the US cotton market opened quietly, and all transactions were of a liquidation nature. The High Court's ruling will be announced on Monday, so both sides were engaged in reselling and repurchasing, with a relatively solid actual position. Prices rose due to buying by peers, but selling in the South caused the market to soften later as long positions were liquidated and New Orleans sold off. Increased textile sales indicate demand for goods from buyers, and factories also need cotton. The market closed weak, with spot prices unchanged and futures prices falling by 2-8 points. British cotton spot prices fell by 9 points, and futures prices fell by 4-5 points. Indian cotton fell due to large-scale selling by operators and scattered selling by European exporters. Prices subsequently weakened due to long liquidation and negative news from Liverpool. Pingor fell by 2 rupees, Oomra fell by 3-3.25 rupees, and White Rose fell by 3.25 rupees. On Snow

— (Wei Jing)

The phenomenon of snow is truly peculiar. Snow that falls in winter is hexagonal, perfectly symmetrical, with each flake being identical. As it falls, it appears dry, and if it lands on you, a gentle brush of the hand easily removes it. However, snow that falls in spring is vastly different. Each snowflake is irregular, with some petals missing and others indistinct. As it falls, it melts easily. If it lands on clothing, it quickly turns into a drop of water. Although spring officially begins at Shen Shi (3-5 PM) today, snow falling before Wei Shi (1-3 PM) still exhibits the form and characteristics of winter snow. Snow falling at Xu Shi (7-9 PM) or Hai Shi (9-11 PM) takes on a completely different appearance, entirely characteristic of spring snow. Why is there such a clear distinction between winter and spring snow? I haven't found it discussed in science books, but I believe it's likely due to the different climate after the change of seasons.

According to common knowledge in our village, winter snow benefits agricultural products. The reason is that the cold of the snow can penetrate the dense soil, freezing to death any harmful insects or their egg masses that have burrowed into the soil in the autumn. Therefore, the more winter snow falls, the happier the farmers are, saying that "six-petaled snowflakes flying presage a bountiful year." As for spring snow, it is the farmer's great enemy because it can cause the tender wheat roots to rot. Therefore, I hope that Heaven sends down more snow this winter. Let the snow that is meant to fall next spring be finished off this winter.

Interpretation of Ancient Proverbs About Snow

— Hua Ling

When the weather is cold and the ground freezes, it is inevitable that snow will fall, and the editor of this column will naturally have to produce a "Snow Special Edition" to fit the occasion. So, I have taken two ancient proverbs about snow that were at hand, added new interpretations, and expanded them into an article to fill the blank space.

Snow Lion Facing Fire: "Snow lion facing fire" means unable to withstand. This is exactly like the current dating process of ordinary men and women. Unmarried women in their boudoirs are seeking sexual gratification. At this moment, as long as there is a man who is good at flattery and enticement, they will be unable to restrain themselves like a snow lion facing fire and will inevitably engage in unmentionable improprieties. At the same time, a virgin who has never had sexual relations with any woman, once he enters the world of feminine wiles, will be seduced by a woman who is used to romance, and he will become as limp as a lion facing the fire, at the mercy of others and unable to extricate himself.

In international affairs, we can also associate it with a small African country that actually dares to discuss war with a powerful nation. Its situation is clearly like a snow lion facing fire. But now the League of Nations is using collective force to sanction Italy. Italy, with its national strength, is confronting the whole world, and judging by the situation, it naturally seems a bit like a snow lion facing fire.

Sending Charcoal in the Snow: In ancient times, everything was said to be kind, but even then, there were few who sent charcoal in the snow. In these times, the world is falling apart, and the contrast between warmth and coldness is becoming increasingly sharp. Everyone is only looking out for their own interests. There are plenty who add flowers to brocade, but you can't find one or two who send charcoal in the snow out of a hundred. Those with wealth and power, with their thirtieth birthday, the old man's eightieth birthday, as soon as there is an action, there are many who follow the trend and flatter them. What about those who have lost power? When they go bankrupt and jump into the sea, everyone just laughs coldly at them. Someone who is willing to say a word or two of sympathy is already very kind. Anyone who is willing to send charcoal in the snow and provide assistance will be laughed at as the number one fool in the world. Look, most of the starving disaster victims are still waiting to die in the frozen world. From this, we can see how few people send charcoal in the snow.

As for international affairs, isn't it the same? If you don't have the strength yourself, don't even think about anyone being willing to speak up for justice. The powerful, at most, only sweep the snow in front of their own doors, who is willing to send charcoal in the snow?

A Sunny Morning After the Snow

Snow Musings

— Zhou Xian

After it snows, the happiest creatures are dogs, who love to run around on the snow. Each step leaves deep, plum-blossom-shaped footprints on the snow. At the same time, sparrows are unfortunately out of luck, as the ground's food is covered in white snow, causing them to chirp and squawk incessantly. Hence, the proverb "Snow makes dogs happy, sparrows angry" (perhaps the sparrows are also singing the praises of snow, but alas, the tongue of man knows not bird-speech, so we cannot prove it).

Children also welcome snow very much, throwing snowballs, building snowmen and snow lions, which is all good fun. When I was young, I also loved to play in the snow, and was often scolded by my parents for it. When I grew a little older, I realized that adults also love snow. Visiting plum blossoms in the snow, and composing poems about the snow are considered to be quite refined activities. In the "Rhyme Dictionary," there are so many references to snow. Since ancient times, there have been so many poems about snow that one could read them for three days and three nights without finishing. From this, one can know that adults' love of snow is no less than that of children.

In "The Story of the Stone," the eccentric Miss Miaoyu, residing outside the fold, collects snowflakes from plum blossoms in the winter, seals them, and stores them underground to brew pre-rain tea, and doesn't allow commoners to taste it, which is naturally a unique practice of the Buddhist sect. But in my hometown, old women would store winter snow water, treating it as a precious commodity, claiming that it could cure eye diseases, relieve throat pain, and even heal typhoid fever. Although this is a form of waste utilization, it is not mentioned in the medical book that Hua Tuo the doctor's wife burned, so I feel it's not something to be emulated.

Of course, all of the above is from before the 20th century. But the white snow, following the times, is still very popular today. Look, the 20th-century new poets, specializing in new-style poems, are still chanting about the snow. Mechanical photographers also get their cameras out and get to work when it snows. Artists who have returned from Rome and Paris also love to put snow scenes on canvas.

Also, it seems that snow is not only welcomed by gentlemen, but to put it in a distorted way, "elder sisters" and "aunties," and "silk factory girls," treat "snow-white" skin creams as their second life. If you praise a woman by saying "her skin is as white as snow," she will be happy from the bottom of her heart, and acknowledge you as someone who knows a good thing when they see it.

Snow Morning

— Bo Guang

Yesterday afternoon, the sky was covered with dark clouds, and the temperature on the thermometer suddenly dropped. After dinner, large, goose-feather-like snowflakes fell, and the shops closed their doors earlier than usual. My wife, the child and I huddled in the room, warming ourselves by the stove, and did not feel too cold. The next day, I was still in bed and dawn had not yet broken. Although I was covered with a silk quilt, the cold was pressing in fiercely! The bed was warm, and I was reluctant to get up. But the sunlight was already shining through the glass window, and looking out with the sunlight, the snow on the roof was exceptionally white and pleasing! I sat up in bed, washed and dressed, and after breakfast, I was reading a newspaper. Hanmei sent me an invitation card, inviting me to a snow viewing party at ten o'clock, with hot pot and warm wine. This was wonderful, especially since the weather was so clear.

There were a total of ten people at the party. Hanmei, the host, made the following suggestion: "I will give you a first line, and if you can't come up with a second line, each of you will be fined an old cotton coat. We think of the compatriots in the disaster area, crying from hunger and cold. It is so pitiful, with the cruel winter, the dripping water freezes, and there is such a heavy snow. When we are drinking and warm, we should put ourselves in the position of our compatriots in the disaster area! If we don't help them, won't they freeze to death?" Having said that, he gave us the first line, "Snow falls on the plank bridge, chickens and dogs pass, forming the shape of bamboo leaves and plum blossoms." Wang Jun proposed: "Let's assume our learning is shallow and each of us contribute a cotton coat." The others agreed, and it was decided to hand over the clothes to the People's Education Center to be delivered to the disaster area.

In such cold snowy weather, people with money should donate money to help, and those without money should donate a few clothes as well. It is hoped that people will actively contribute!

A Snow Story

— Shou Qiu

The weather is cold! The snowflakes have started to flutter! This has motivated me to write this article:

"Cold before frost, cold after snow." These are two Chinese proverbs. But let us not underestimate these two proverbs, they are very scientific. We know that after it snows, the weather will definitely get colder, so the poor people often shout that it is terrible! But on the other hand, snow is something that is beneficial to people. According to the term "auspicious snow" and the idiom "snow foretells a good year," we can know that snow is a good thing. If there is no snowfall in winter, that is terrible!

Speaking of snow, I am reminded of a story! This happened a couple of years ago. It is said that there was a family who sold wine in a certain place. This year, they could not afford to sell wine, so they had a lot of empty jars piled up at home, during the winter. It happened to snow heavily, and the wine seller, because he was so cold, used a spoon to scoop the hard snow into the empty jars. He scooped like this a few times, and he managed to fill more than a hundred jars! He was just playing around temporarily, and using this to resist the cold. Who knew that things would turn out unexpectedly. In the late spring and early summer of the following year, the area suddenly encountered an unprecedented drought. The rich people were holding silver dollars (at that time, the currency had not yet been reformed) and had nowhere to buy water. Just when they were very panic-stricken, the wine seller remembered the snow stored in the jars. He hurriedly opened one and looked, and it had turned into very clear water. So he leaked the news that he was selling each jar for one silver dollar. The rich people knew that it was snow water, and it was not easy to get, so they all rushed to send people to buy it. In less than two days, he had sold them all! He—the wine seller—also made a small fortune, which became his capital. This is the story of making a fortune from snow, but it is something that can only be met and not sought!

Little Western Paradise

— By Zhang Henshui

Episode 23: Engaging in Lofty Discussions in the Room, Rising Up to Sue; Pouring Wine, Renewing Old Friendships, Forgetting Grievances for Profit

Today, Jia Duocai was surrounded by these female heroes. He used every trick he knew, both tough and soft, but nothing worked against them. His anger was so great he wished he could cut off his head to vent it. Now, seeing Wang Beihai standing aside, also mocking him with words, he couldn't contain his rage. He glared at him and asked, "Who are you? How dare you offend me with your words? Let me tell you, I'm not someone to be bullied."

Beihai seemed to have prepared a speech. He tugged at his collar, still smiling, and replied in a very gentle tone, "Mr. Jia, I recognize you. I know you're from the banking world. I won't argue with you. Perhaps I'm being kind, reminding you with my words. If you're trying to pick a fight with me, I'll let you win. You can say I'm afraid of you, and it wouldn't be wrong. I hope you can show that same fearless spirit when dealing with those ladies."

Saying that, he chuckled loudly, raised his right hand, shrunk his body, and retreated to the backyard. Jia Duocai stood in the reception hall, somewhat stunned. However, recalling Beihai's late arrival, he suddenly understood, thinking, "Could it be that troublesome guest has left?" He immediately ran to the room to look around, but no one was there. Sitting in a chair, he thought for a moment and then repeatedly slapped the table, calling for the tea boy.

The tea boy, seeing Yueying go upstairs, was already feeling uneasy about the situation. Now, hearing Jia Duocai calling out in such a chaotic manner, he blushed and entered. Jia Duocai pressed his hand on the table, jumped up, and asked, "Where's my wife?"

Just then, a burst of laughter came from outside the window. He put his hands on his hips, glared with wide eyes, and looked at the tea boy. The tea boy said in a low voice, "Your wife went upstairs to Commissioner Lan's wife's place." He answered very cautiously, keeping his hands at his sides and his head slightly lowered.

Jia Duocai said, "Go upstairs and call her back. Tell her this is a place of trouble, and I want to leave." The tea boy refused to leave, answering in a low voice, "I'm afraid I can't persuade her. Mrs. Lan said she was afraid Mr. Jia would want her back, so she's keeping her here." (387)

Observations

— (Ziming)

Snowflakes, like silver, fluttered and danced, adorning our land with a peculiar charm. The weather was piercingly cold, but the patriotic fervor of students in various regions was surging in inverse proportion. Students at a certain school were, of course, no exception; however, their movement was without freedom, constantly monitored and restricted. Their inner resentment burned even more strongly.

Dozens of students, in a flurry of activity, piled the snow on the ground into many snowmen. This snowman was a certain traitor, that snowman was a certain collaborator, all labeled with names; and the faces they made were indeed strikingly similar to the people they labeled. The students then armed themselves, taking wooden guns or broadswords, and chopped off the heads of the snowmen, hanging them at the school gate, as if to show all the traitors to the public.

This kind of foolish action may be close to being like Ah Q; but it also reveals the students' patriotic enthusiasm and degree of resentment.

Medical Lecture

An Introduction to Gonorrhea

— Doctor Feng Shanliang

After gonococci invade the human body, in males, they lurk in the folds of the urethral mucosa, and in females, they lurk in the glands of the cervical canal. This kind of gonococcal proliferation can continue throughout one's life. Therefore, intercourse with someone who has this disease will inevitably lead to transmission, with very few exceptions. When gonococci first invade the male genitalia, it is usually acute anterior urethritis. When gonococci invade the female genitalia, due to the complexity of the organ structure, sometimes adjacent organs are also affected.

This disease should be treated early, the earlier the better, otherwise, men infect women, and women infect men, creating an endless cycle of infection. However, one should be careful in choosing a doctor, so that the treatment is appropriate, strictly adhering to hygiene, so as not to hinder the healing process. Treatment must be proper and reasonable, such as shortwave diathermy, mixed gonococcal vaccine immunotherapy, "gonococcicide" oral medication, and "Gono-Serol" injection. Combining these methods can be said to be absolute treatment. With such treatment, there is no reason for gonorrhea not to be cured.

— Physician She Lei

Those addicted to opium often have impaired physical health due to long-term exposure to opium toxins. Their physical strength is inferior to that of ordinary people. Therefore, at the beginning of withdrawal, one must first pay attention to their physical strength, that is, nutrition, and be careful in selecting nutritious foods. Then, physical strength can be improved, and the path to quitting smoking can be smooth.

Otherwise, if one does not consider the physical strength of the person quitting, pain will appear immediately after withdrawal, and there will be no good results. This can be stated with certainty. Regardless of the method used to quit smoking, nutritious foods such as milk, eggs, young chicken broth, beef broth, fresh vegetables, and fruits are all suitable. Medications used to increase the physical strength of those quitting smoking, such as egg yolk lecithin, various vitamins, Cerebro-Spinal Tonic, deer antler essence, various endocrine fluids, arsenic-iron iodide preparations, etc., all have considerable value. Other aspects, such as the conditioning of the nerves and gastrointestinal tract, are essential and cannot be ignored. This is because the physical weakness of those addicted to opium is very obvious.

While gradually eliminating the addiction, one should also gradually increase their physical strength. Then, those quitting will have no adverse reactions to the lack of opium's anesthetic effect. Any discomfort will only be mental. Quitting smoking in this way will be a peaceful experience.

Gonorrhea is easily transmitted but difficult to cure. This is because gonococci are constantly lurking in the inner layer of the urethral mucosa. Ordinary medications cannot easily penetrate deep enough. The medications usually used to treat gonorrhea are either oral or topical. Other medications for gonorrhea, such as Copaiba and sandalwood oil, are not only ineffective but also irritate the kidneys and harm the gastrointestinal tract, so one should try to avoid using them.

In my clinical practice, I want to find a reasonable oral medication for treating gonorrhea that has no side effects and is truly effective. Is "Mesaltropin" the answer? The excellence of this medicine can be confirmed by the fact that it is favored by doctors at home and abroad. Regardless of whether the bacteria are encapsulated or hidden deep in the folds of the mucosa, the medicine can penetrate the membrane layer and directly act on the bacteria to kill them.

As for topical medications, silver proteinate and potassium permanganate are usually used as topical washes for treating gonorrhea. However, the bactericidal and membrane-penetrating abilities of these medications are not accurate. What is favored by the medical community nowadays is "Gono-Serol." Talk

The Brutality of Italian Aircraft

— Fang Yin

Just as people were celebrating the New Year with great excitement, a shocking tragedy came from East Africa, reporting that the Swedish Red Cross rescue team had been bombed by Italian aircraft. According to a dispatch from the capital of Abyssinia on New Year's Eve, "Our reporter, Ochanert, reports that several Italian aircraft flew to the Dora area on the southern Wolga Den front line and dropped bombs, destroying all the buildings of the Swedish Red Cross service team there. All the members of the team, except for the leader, Dr. Hilante, were killed. One nurse and one assistant were not killed, but were seriously injured. ..."

As soon as this tragedy spread, public opinion around the world was in uproar. The Surgeon General of the Swedish Army declared: "The Italian army did not do such evil during the European War." Some bishops even said, "The honor of the whole world is feared to be tarnished by this tragedy." Newspapers in the Swedish capital issued extra editions, "Crowds of people thronged the streets, immediately held demonstrations, expressed opposition to Italy, and hundreds of people gathered in front of the Italian embassy, and in a fit of anger, some people punched and waved their arms." The King of Abyssinia also notified the League of Nations one day, protesting the inhumane violence of Italian aircraft.

The Italian imperialist war of aggression against Abyssinia is vociferously "promoting culture" for the white race. The result of this "promotion of culture" is that the Abyssinian people and the wilderness of East Africa are devastated by the "civilized" artillery fire of the white race, and the black people of Abyssinia are trampled upon by Italian imperialism in the same way as India. The world is watching this cruel resistance of a semi-colony against imperialist aggression and sympathizing with Abyssinia for this indomitable anti-resistance sentiment. And the Swedish and other countries' Red Cross rescue teams' going to East Africa to rescue the wounded soldiers of Abyssinia is precisely a clear manifestation of this great sympathy. These Italian aircraft, ignoring the criticism of general opinion and the aversion of the world's people, in addition to "promoting" the people of Abyssinia, also bombed the innocent Swedish rescue team, which clearly exposed the essence of the so-called "promotion of culture" by Italian imperialists.

No matter how the Italian fascists try to argue that this was a "punishment" of the Abyssinians by "Italian military aircraft" and that "there was no intention to harm the Swedish Red Cross," facts speak louder than words, and the hideous face of the Italian fascists has been revealed in this brutality.

The Spoken Drama in China in the Year 24

— Ke Ming

"From now on, spoken drama will be eliminated!"

The person who said this felt that sound movies not only possessed the advantages of spoken drama, such as voice and dialogue, but could also overcome the limitations of time and space imposed on spoken drama. Naturally, this statement is not without reason, but anyone who truly understands art would not say such a thing.

In the realm of art, the relationship between spoken drama and film is like that between poetry and novels, painting and photography—each has its own inherent differences and unique advantages. The emergence of novels does not lead to the demise of poetry, nor does the invention of photography lead to the extinction of painting. Rather, because of the new emergence, both will gradually abandon their respective strengths and weaknesses, complementing each other and advancing to higher stages of art.

The spoken drama movement of the year 24 did not decline and disappear due to the emergence of Chinese sound movies. On the contrary, the booming phenomenon of the spoken drama movement this year is astonishing. Not only in its vigorous atmosphere, but also in the establishment of new techniques derived from new content, further consolidating the value of spoken drama in the realm of art.

The flourishing of the theatrical movement in the year 24 owes considerable credit to the Shanghai Stage Association's performances of "Song of Rejuvenation" and "Under the Mercury Light" at the beginning of the year. Not only were the Melo and entertainment aspects of the plays themselves tailored to the tastes of ordinary small town residents, but the "personal appearances" of more than twenty movie stars, large and small, were indeed enough to create box office records for spoken drama. The convenience of renting theaters for subsequent public performances by several theater groups, and the slight improvement in business, owe no small debt to the former.

Although the script of "Song of Rejuvenation" suited the tastes of the petty bourgeois audience, excessive romanticism not only diluted the anti-imperialist fervor into a faint brushstroke, but the superficial narration and excessive emphasis on entertainment did not achieve a deeper harvest in terms of performance effect. Zhao Dan's earnest acting earned much praise, and Yuan Muzhi's makeup and small gestures were also praised by the general public.

Page 18

It's a pity that he stole the show from others.

However, in "Under the Mercury Light," Yuan Muzhi's calm and refined acting not only lacked the aforementioned shortcomings, but also made a significant contribution to the overall success of the play. His contribution should be considered half of it.

Here, in addition to inheriting the excessive romanticism of "Song of Rejuvenation," the lengthy dialogue describing past history destroyed the atmosphere of the entire play.

Generally speaking, the directing skills can be said to be passable, although some minor flaws remain, such as the disorganization of the scene in the second act of "Song of Rejuvenation."

The film "Smilin' Through," starring Norma Shearer and Leslie Howard, was adapted from the stage play "Fresh Paint," which was publicly performed by the Jinan Drama Society.

Although "Fresh Paint" had the efforts of the director and a lighthearted script, it failed to fully grasp the emotions of the Chinese audience due to differences in living environment. The stiffness of the lines and the triviality of the actions of two or three actors further damaged the overall effect of the play. Shu Yan was quite skilled, but Wang Ying, who played the role equivalent to Norma Shearer, failed to express the demeanor that an old maid should have in her movements and makeup.

The play "L'Arlésienne" by the Qingzhong Drama Society also failed to be fully understood by the general audience due to differences in living environment. The lack of colloquialism in the dialogue was also a fatal flaw. Fortunately, Gu Er'yi's captain and Zhu Mingxian's mother slightly enlivened the whole play.

A prerequisite for acting in spoken drama is the naturalness of the dialogue and the clear distinction between high and low tones, but the "Midsummer Night's Dream" performed by Qingxin Girls' High School did not possess this condition. The gorgeous costumes did not compensate for the unfamiliarity of the whole play.

John Drama Society's "The White Haired Girl" easily won some success in performance due to the terror, comic relief, and low-grade趣味 inherent in the script. Although "Freedom" deeply portrayed four different personalities, the unfamiliarity of the actors and their lack of deep understanding of the characters meant that the effect of the performance depended on "The White Haired Girl." The familiar "Thief," with the help of lighting and scenery, was still able to capture the emotions of the audience.

The "Storm on the Yangtze" and "Three Sisters" performed by Peiming Girls' High School did not achieve higher success. "Oppression" received considerable praise due to the lighthearted script and the efforts of actors such as Shen Ruchen, although it was far inferior to the former in meaning. "A Doll's House (Nora)," which was performed in Nanjing and then in Shanghai, was first performed at the Guanghua Affiliated High School, and the overall effect of the play achieved limited success. The director did not handle the whole play in an orderly manner, and although Kang Zhang worked hard, she did not fully understand the personalities of the characters.

Fudan Drama Society's "Compromise" achieved completeness in both the script itself and the performance techniques. The director's efforts were evident in the small gestures and the grand settings, and actors such as Feng Zi and Gu De'gang were very competent. Although it was also a satirical comedy, it was much better at manipulating the audience's emotions than "Fresh Paint" because of its proximity to life.

"Friends in Trouble," "Chastity," and "Farewell" were the three plays performed by the Ma Yi Drama Society in its second public performance. The selection of the scripts and the effect of the performances were not as successful as expected.

The "Modern Lady" performed at the Shanghai Theater was not significantly different in form from the general stage plays recently performed in China. Unfortunately, the director was contaminated with a bit of the style of early Chinese "spoken drama," although actors such as Hong Ying worked hard. The main idea of the whole play was to persuade modernized women to return to the family. The author's painstaking effort was to improve people's hearts.

Although amateur actors performed the familiar play "A Doll's House (Nora)" for the first time, this play is worth performing again and again in the current situation where women are not allowed to enter society.

The dedication and effort of the director and actors made the performance of the whole play a great success. The acting skills of Lan Ping, Zhao Dan, and Jin Shan here also received widespread praise.

Although "Hero and Beauty" is a very good satirical play, the Jizhong Drama Society did not make enough effort. The messy settings, stiff movements, and forced dialogue ruined the entire play.

The Hua Hua Drama Society, which wanted to improve business by renaming "Dunce" as "The Merry Widow" and performing it, had unexpectedly dismal box office results. In terms of form, it was almost completely Peking Opera-ized.

The "Xi Shi" performed by the Shanghai Theater for the second time was also almost completely Peking Opera-ized in form.

The "Moon Bends" performed by the Star Film Company almost completely inherited the techniques used in the first performance of the Shanghai Theater.

The Experimental Drama Troupe's performances of "The Miser" and "Oppression" did not achieve anything good either.

John Drama Society also performed "Returning South," "Friends in Trouble," and "Tunnel," but it seems that they did not pay careful attention to stage techniques.

Among the satirical comedies publicly performed in the year 24, "Untitled" was the most commendable in terms of its positive significance. In particular, the help of the sound effects and the sudden change of lighting at the end added a lot of color to the whole play. Except that the overall tone was not bright enough, the whole play was hilarious from beginning to end. Gu Er'yi's magistrate, Lan Ping's carpenter's wife, and Ye Luxi's daughter were all very skilled. Jin Shan seemed unable to fully fit the personality of the character in the play, and although Wang Ying worked hard, she still maintained the style she had in "Fresh Paint."

Fudan Drama Society's four-act tragedy "Thunderstorm" also made considerable achievements. The playwright used a deep and tragic tone to expose the ugliness of a large family. The director also put a lot of effort into the small gestures, and actors such as Hu Nianzhong and Feng Zi were very dedicated.

Qiazhong Girls' High School performed "One Night in a Northeastern Girls' Dormitory." In the current Chinese situation, this play is the most worthy of recommendation. It pointed out the future path for the students, and at the same time sharply satirized student life. The performance was still barely satisfactory.

This is a very general and rough record of the spoken drama movement in the year 24. Errors and omissions are inevitable. The liveliness and vigor of spoken drama in the year 24 are commendable and gratifying. Although some nondescript things are mixed in, that is unavoidable on the road of development. The creation of new content and the establishment of new techniques resulting from new content have rapidly advanced the backward Chinese spoken drama to another higher stage. Now that the national crisis is deepening day by day and the patriotic and saving movement is expanding day by day, recognize the duty you should fulfill in your own field and redouble your efforts, friends who are engaged in spoken drama!

Singing Girl

— Meng Hua

When the street lights begin to shine brightly, a group of young girls dressed in gaudy clothes appear outside the bustling Qianmen gate.

They are engaged in the business of singing. As soon as the sun sets, they take off their tattered short shirts and change into a set of brand new clothes, apply snow-white fragrant powder on their yellow and thin faces, smear fragrant and smooth pomade on their disheveled hair, and dab bright rouge on their withered lips. They stroll gracefully onto the streets, going in and out of the brothels in the Eight Great Hutongs, enticing guests to buy their songs, subjected to the guests' lewd teasing and ridicule, the girls' contemptuous glances and insults... until late at night, they drag their weary steps back home. These little girls, living what appears to be a rosy life but is actually gray and white, are the singing girls who visit hundreds of doors.

Sixi Zi has been doing this business for more than two years. She started following her grandfather in this business at the age of fourteen. Whether it was winter or summer, whether it was snowing or raining, she went out every day from dark and did not return home until late at night, when the father and daughter walked back home like two ghosts in the dark alley.

"Sixi'er, hurry up and dress up, you think it's still early, don't you?" It was her mother's voice, speaking with a reproachful air.

"Mom, wouldn't it be nice if you let me rest for one night? We earn enough money to make a living," Sixi'er threw the work in her hand into the sewing basket and stood up to say this.

"Sixi'er, you're not young anymore, and you should share some of Mom's worries," her mother's voice softened a little. "Mom is telling you, don't make your dad angry, be good, and go. It's getting late."

Sixi'er didn't speak, picked up the work, and lowered her head to continue.

"Your grandfather is so old, but he's still the same. Has he ever taken a day off? You, you should still go!" Her mother seemed to be pleading. "In a while, I'll ask your sister to help you out. When she learns, you won't have to go out anymore."

"In a while, it's always in a while, when will it be?" Sixi'zi rolled her eyes, glaring at her mother. "I won't go, I'd rather die than go, I'd rather starve to death. We'll never suffer this hardship again!"

Her mother was stunned and couldn't say a word. She knew that doing this business was hard, and her daughter was growing up. She felt distressed in her heart when she was subjected to the guests' lewd teasing, but what could she do? Since her dad has been idle, doesn't the family's food, clothing, and supplies depend on Sixi'er's mouth? After a pause, she persuaded again,

"Good child, listen to Mom! Any hardship is worth enduring. If you don't go, won't you let your dad and Mom starve to death? Don't let your dad hear you, or he'll start arguing again."

"Endure! Endure, do you know what it's like? People touch you and touch you, and you have to let them do whatever they want for a few cents? What's the difference between us and the girls in the 'lower places' (a name for the lowest-grade brothels in Beiping)? And now this market, there aren't many people listening in the 'lower places.' Although there are more in the 'tea houses,' the gatekeepers want a tip for opening the door (a kind of extra money for the doorman), not even a penny less. Even if your business is good, you go to ten or twenty places, and you shout until your voice is hoarse, but you don't end up with much money. The girls in the group are good at getting good things from the guests' hands, and they always say that the rewards are too much, and they have to deduct from it. And..." Sixi'er said here, tears fell down her face, and her chest convulsed violently. Then, she rubbed her chest hard with her hands, while saying intermittently:

"And those bastards... When they see you... A slap on the right side,... a kick on the left,... twisting your hair... giving you a whip... to eat,... look," she pointed to the purplish-black bruise on her arm, "it wasn't just from them twisting me last night: Mom... Mom, I'd rather die than go out, I... I... work at home..." Sixi'zi couldn't say anymore, lifted her skirt to wipe her tears, and coughed dryly, unable to breathe.

"Xi'er, don't say it, Mom loves you," the mother's voice was also a little hoarse.

Just then, her dad ran out, coughing and panting.

"Xi'er, I'm telling you, isn't everything in the world the same? When I used to work for the opera troupe, I suffered even more than you! That is to say, they are people who have something, do you know? Which rich person doesn't use their power, doesn't look for fun? Otherwise, what are they doing in the brothels? You always have to endure some things. If you don't go, we'll have to tighten our belts tomorrow! Alas, I only blame my bones for being hard. Now it's a famine year. Otherwise, I wouldn't let my own daughter be played with by others, played with in front of me, you say..."

"Enough! You always say endure, endure, endure. When will we stop enduring? Aren't people all made the same way? Why do we have to be played with by them? Can't we just starve to death if we do other businesses? Tell me, have you ever suffered those hardships?"

"Okay!" Sixi'zi threw away the work in her hand and stopped crying, shouting loudly. "Okay, we'll take one more trip tonight. If anyone touches me, I'll slap them in the face. If I ruin the business, don't blame me."

"Doing this kind of thing isn't human, hey:..." Sixi'zi took off her outer shirt and walked into the room angrily.

When the street lights began to shine brightly, a group of young girls dressed in gaudy clothes appeared outside the bustling Qianmen gate. Among them, there was Sixi'zi.

Brought Good News

— Especially

—Nostalgia for a Bitter Snow, Part 3—

Loneliness, on the solitary, may be appropriate, no, for one of leisurely taste, it can indeed regulate the spleen and stomach, for a wandering person whose heartstrings have been burned by fire, for a wanderer overwhelmed by all the suffering and melancholy, loneliness, that is not needed, in the silence where all sounds are quiet, it can bring endless troubles, sorrows, all into the brain, revolving, revolving, like a zoetrope, at the same time, a merciless arrow will unceremoniously pierce straight into the chest.

Don't you not want to be lonely? This thought cannot be done, every day, opening your eyes, the sky always seems to have immense sorrow, pulling down a bitter face, in a small room with only one window, shrouded all day in dreary clouds, there is no smile on each person's face. In the morning, scrambling out of the covers, casually wiping a face, clutching a hopeful mood, hurriedly going their separate ways.

What about me? This is difficult, not being the person in charge, one might even be treated as a greenhorn by the person in charge, everything, naturally, must be subject to the orders of others. Wanting to go out to change the stuffy air, unfamiliar with the route, and the snow is so heavy, it will bury your feet. Although a greenhorn would not get lost, the face of the person in charge is not good to look at after all.

Contacting, unblocking, busy coming forward all day, the hopeful mood, when brought back, is a lump of frustration. When the oil lamp is placed in front of our faces, there is almost always a burst of complaints.

-How was it when you went to see Commander × today?

-Difficult, all official language, nothing was indicated.

-Then, Lao Wei said: are we just going to stop here and not leave?

-Leave? Who has this way, we already knew, this departure was an adventure.

A cloud of thick smoke separated everyone, in the thick smoke, everyone quieted down!

The charcoal fire was burning brightly, the ice surface already formed in the courtyard, groaning and creaking with the footsteps of passers-by.

-I really don't believe there will be one, who would squat in the no man's land of Zhengzhou.

Brother, don't talk, now you should believe it, everything, can never be affirmed in ideals.

-Damn it, I was still saying that I would rush back to Tianjin to celebrate the New Year on the 28th or 29th!

Lao Liu glanced at Xiao Wei's face and said faintly: "Forget it, before the New Year, the sister-in-law doesn't have the good fortune to get your warmth.

Laughter spread from one person to the whole group, Xiao Wei's face was not thick after all, and he couldn't help but blush.

Xiao Wei is a young man full of enthusiasm, married for just three or four months, for the sake of life, the whip drove him to this twilight ancient city, if in an unintentional moment, one mentioned their own woman to each other, then he, would滔滔不絕narrate her merits, his heart itching, and his face would follow and turn red.

-Tomorrow, really, I'll go to ××× and ask him to think of a way, Xiao Wei said, if it doesn't work, we'll still go back, don't wait here anymore. You have to spend money, you have to socialize, if there's no money, we'll just wait to die!

Of course, we are happy to accept this proposal, for the sake of convenience in speaking, we had to ask Xiao Wei to bother.

The next day, the fiery red sun shone on the east, the sky was a clear mirror, the accumulated snow, daring not to resist as usual, the texture melted, dripping and dripping, the dirt road on the street was muddy and slippery.

Maybe today can bring us good news? The sky, in bringing a symbol of glory. I thought in my heart.

The air in the room was the same as before, lonely, I guarded the lamplight and looked through the news of the day, letting the time slip by on every small character and every paragraph of advertisement. Later, they came back, and as soon as they entered the door, they brought unusual joy.

——Oh, how much explanation it took, we finally have a definite date, we're setting off on the 25th, the day to go home for the New Year won't be delayed哟! He shouted wildly, laughed, and his passionate eyes were a little charming.

A table of dishes was ordered, the good news, rippling in everyone's heart. I don't know who suggested it, but two more flower girls were called to pour wine. Passion, revelry, everything was forgotten in the revelry.

All the hopes, tightly fastened to the galloping of the vehicles, counting down, there should still be a week of stay!

Opening: "Xiang Ling Asks After Illness"

Vast twilight gradually descends. The rustling breeze and fine rain drizzle. Dim and silent is Xiang Ling's abode. Desolate and lingering are the shadows of slender bamboos. The carefree master of Yi Hong is a man of passion. He thinks of the melancholic, sickly woman. Wearing his bamboo hat and raincoat, he hurriedly carries a lantern through the garden. Arriving at the Xiaoxiang Pavilion, the lady has just put down her brush, ceasing her poetry. A maid suddenly announces the arrival of the Second Master. He appears, dressed in a manner different from usual. "Brother Bao, why do you imitate the attire of a fisherman?" The master, hearing this, quickly inquires, "Is Sister's health peaceful? Has your medicine been taken? Has your appetite improved? You mustn't write poetry these days. My heart is constantly burdened, hence I brave the rain to inquire." "If Sister likes this attire, I shall send her a set on a pleasant day." Qing replies, "Why would I need such a thing? The image of a fisherwoman is meaningless." As the words leave her lips, she ponders. "Fisherman and fisherwoman should not be mentioned." Her peach blossom face flushes with uncontainable shame. Silently, she lowers her head, not uttering a sound. One unintentionally misspoke. The other has not heard the truth, how would she know the feelings? The Dream of the Red Chamber is full of changes and illusions. Briefly depicting that, Xiang Ling inquired after illness, a marital fate. I hate that the old man in the moon does not draw a thread of love. Hence, medicine is always ineffective. In vain do they bear a mutual affection.

A new era of equal rights dawns. Together, they work in the commercial arena. Its scale is grand and extraordinary. The recruitment conditions for female office workers require beauty, youth, and elegant demeanor. Her clothes and jewelry have all been pawned. Fortunately, the child is lively. A pearl in her palm, loved beyond compare. She apprehensively applies to the company. After a few days, her name appears at the top of the list in the newspaper. She diligently works, arriving every day. Complex Layout of "Wedding Night"

"Wedding Night" is a film that focuses on marriage problems, depicting the secret affairs between men and women in society and exploring the impact of these affairs on family organization. In other words, it is a social drama that deals with marital problems. In the middle of this, it includes sacred love, money love, power love, and master-servant love. The playwright delicately describes and narrates the best he can, and the director handles it in an orderly manner and is extremely skillful. Now a brief description of its layout is given below: (Note: For easy understanding, the names of the actors are used)

Lin Ling is a romantic and unrestrained modern woman, and also the wife of the writer Wang Yin, but she cannot accept Wang Yin's sincere love, and instead goes to love the playboy Zhang Baili. (This is money love) Later, Wang Yin, in frustration, accidentally meets Yuan Meiyun. The two admire each other and finally fall in love (this is sacred love). However, Yuan Meiyun has already been promised to someone else, and although she struggles repeatedly, she gains nothing. As a result, under the pressure of tyrannical power, she marries Guan Hongda with grief and tears. (This is power love) Zhou Xuan is the maid used by the Guan family. She loves Guan Hongda most sincerely. (This is master-servant love) There is a book boy in the Guan family named Liu Li, who wholeheartedly loves Zhou Xuan. (This is the love between servants)

"Wedding Night" has the above complex layout. As for what the result will be, only "Wedding Night" will tell you clearly.

Young Composer Sha Mei Holds Children's Art Song Concert

The musical theories of young composer Mr. Sha Mei have long been admired by the public. In recent years, Mr. Sha has especially worked hard on composition. His works such as "On the Jialing River" and "Blacksmith Song" have been well received by the public since they were published in the Electronic Communications Pictorial, and have a strong Nie Er style. It is said that Mr. Sha plans to publicly perform dozens of children's art songs he has composed in the past year, and the concert will be sung by the children's choir of a British primary school in this city. It is scheduled to be held on the 12th of this month at the Youth Association Auditorium in Ba Xianqiao.
